# 《AI 提示聖經》-The AI Prompt Bible -- Anton Volney

來源: 《AI 提示聖經》-The AI Prompt Bible -- Anton Volney.epub
轉換時間: 2026-02-09 16:11

---

The AI Prompt Bible
AI Prompt Bible 
    

    

      By Anton Volney
      

    


    

      
    

    

      
    

    

      Introduction
導論 
    

    

      Using AI effectively requires more than asking basic questions – the quality and structure of your prompts determine the quality of the results. As one expert noted, 
      “Garbage inputs? Garbage outputs. But if you feed it great inputs—deep insights and powerful prompts—it will evolve into something extraordinary”
      ​
有效使用 AI 不僅僅是提出基本問題，你的提示詞的品質與結構會決定結果的品質。有位專家曾指出：「垃圾輸入？垃圾輸出。但如果你提供優質的輸入—深刻的洞察與強大的提示詞，它將會進化成非凡的東西。」 
    

    

      The difference between an average user and a power user isn’t the AI itself, it’s how they prompt it. 
普通用戶與高階用戶之間的差異不在於 AI 本身，而在於他們如何提示 AI。
    

    

      High-level users treat AI as an interactive collaborator rather than a question-answer machine. Instead of a one-shot query, they provide context, assume roles, or break tasks into steps. 
高階使用者將 AI 視為互動的協作者，而非只是問答機。他們不會只提出一次性的問題，而是提供情境、假設角色，或將任務拆解為步驟。
    

    

      For example, rather than simply asking 
      “Give me business advice,”
       a power user might say: 
      “Act as a veteran CEO mentor. I’ll describe my startup, and you will ask me probing questions before giving advice.”
例如，他們不會只是簡單地問「給我商業建議」，而是可能會說：「請扮演一位資深 CEO 導師。我會描述我的創業公司，你在給建議前先問我一些深入的問題。」
       
    

    

      This richer setup guides the AI to produce a deeper, tailored response​.
這種更豐富的設定能引導 AI 產生更深入且個性化的回應。
    

    

      This reference manual compiles 100+ advanced, high-impact prompts designed for tangible results. 
這本參考手冊收錄了 100 多個高階、高影響力的提示語，旨在帶來實際的成果。
    

    

      The prompts are categorized by domain – primarily Business applications, with dedicated sections for Marketing, Coding, Personal Development, and Creative Writing. 
提示分類依領域而定 – 主要為商業應用，並有專門的章節針對行銷、程式設計、個人發展與創意寫作。 
    

    

      They demonstrate a range of structures: from simple commands to multi-step interactions, employing techniques like role-playing (having the AI assume a persona), Socratic questioning (the AI asks clarifying questions), constraint-based creativity (imposing rules or formats), and iterative refinement (improving answers through feedback). 
它們展示多種結構：從簡單的指令到多步驟的互動，運用技巧如角色扮演（讓 AI 假設某個身分）、蘇格拉底式提問（AI 提出澄清問題）、基於限制的創意（設立規則或格式）以及反覆修正（透過反饋改善回答）。 
    

    

      Each prompt entry includes an explanation and notes on which AI model is best suited for it, considering strengths and weaknesses of GPT-4, GPT-3.5, Claude, Gemini, etc., in different scenarios.
每個提示條目都包含說明，並標註哪種 AI 模型最適合使用，考量 GPT-4、GPT-3.5、Claude、Gemini 等模型在不同情境下的優勢與弱點。 
    

    

      Let’s dive in!
讓我們深入了解一下！
    

    

      General Advanced Prompt Techniques (All Domains)
一般高階提示技巧（所有領域）
    

    

      These prompt structures can be applied to various scenarios or used in combination with domain-specific prompts. They are “meta” techniques that improve the effectiveness of your interactions, ensuring clarity, creativity, and refinement.
這些提示結構可以應用於各種情境，或與特定領域的提示結合使用。它們是「元」技巧，用以提升互動的成效，確保清晰、創意與精緻。
    

    

      Interpretation Check – Verify Instructions
詮釋檢查 – 驗證指示
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Do not start writing yet. First, explain everything I asked you to do in this prompt, in detail, in your own words.”
提示：「不要開始寫作。首先，用你自己的話詳細說明我在此提示中要求你做的事情。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Explicitly asks the AI to paraphrase the task before answering.
技巧 : 明確要求 AI 在回答前先重新表述任務。 
    

    

      Outcome
      : The model summarizes your instructions, confirming it understands your request correctly​. This catches any misinterpretation early, preventing those “that’s not what I meant” moments. You can then correct the AI’s summary if needed, aligning its understanding with your intent.
結果 : 模型會總結你的指示，確認它正確理解你的請求。這能及早發現任何誤解，避免那些「這不是我意思」的尷尬情況。你也可以在需要時修正 AI 的總結，使其理解與你的意圖一致。 
    

    

      Clarifying Questions First (Socratic Prompt)
先提出澄清問題（蘇格拉底提問法） 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “I have a request: [describe task or problem]. If anything is unclear or missing, ask me up to 3 specific clarifying questions before answering. Only provide the solution after I answer your questions.”
提示 : 「我有一個請求：[描述任務或問題]。如果有任何不清楚或遺漏的地方，請在回答前提出最多 3 個具體的澄清問題。只有在我回答你的問題後，才提供解決方案。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Instructs the AI to act like a curious collaborator who uses Socratic questioning. It must diagnose missing info first rather than guessing.
技巧 : 指導 AI 扮演一個好奇的夥伴，使用蘇格拉底式提問。它必須先診斷缺失的資訊，而不是隨意猜測。
    

    

      Outcome
      : The AI will respond with pointed clarifying questions instead of an immediate (and possibly flawed) answer. After you (the user) clarify, the AI can incorporate those details into a much more accurate and tailored solution. This is useful for complex tasks where you might have omitted details. It ensures the final output is based on complete information.
結果 : AI 會以具體的澄清問題來回應，而不是立即（可能有缺陷）給出答案。在你（使用者）澄清後，AI 才能將這些細節納入，提供更準確且符合需求的解決方案。這對於複雜任務特別有用，因為你可能遺漏了一些細節。這確保了最終的輸出是基於完整資訊的。
    

    

      Recommended Model
      : GPT-4 is excellent at asking relevant questions and waiting for input. GPT-3.5 can do this too, though it may sometimes attempt an answer outright – be sure to prompt it firmly. Claude is also strong here, often asking very in-depth clarifying questions given its conversational training. Gemini could leverage its reasoning to identify gaps as well. Use this technique when the task’s requirements aren’t fully specified or when you want the AI to think before it speaks.
建議模型 : GPT-4 在提出相關問題並等待輸入方面表現非常出色。GPT-3.5 也可以做到，不過有時可能會直接嘗試回答 – 請務必清楚地提示它。Claude 在此方面也很強大，由於其對對話的訓練，經常會提出非常深入的澄清問題。Gemini 也可以利用其推理能力來識別資訊缺口。當任務的需求尚未完全明確，或你希望 AI 在回答前先思考時，可以使用此技巧。
    

    

      Step-by-Step Reasoning (Chain-of-Thought)
逐步推理（Chain-of-Thought）
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Let’s work this out step by step. List your reasoning process and calculations (if any), then give the final answer to [the problem].”
讓我們一步一步來思考。列出你的推理過程和計算（如有），然後給出 [問題] 的最終答案。
    

    

      Technique
      : Requests the AI to show its work by breaking down the solution. This is known as chain-of-thought prompting.
技巧：要求 AI 透過分解解決方案來展示其思考過程。這被稱為思維鏈提示法。
    

    

      Outcome
      : The AI provides a logical sequence of steps or thoughts (often numbered or in a narrative form) followed by the answer. For complex problems (math, logic, planning), this often yields more accurate results. 
結果：AI 會提供一個邏輯步驟序列或思考過程（通常為數字編號或敘述形式），然後再給出答案。對於複雜問題（如數學、邏輯、規劃等），這通常能產生更準確的結果。
    

    

      In fact, inserting a phrase like “Let’s think this through step by step” can significantly enhance accuracy on complex reasoning tasks​. You benefit by seeing why the AI answered the way it did, and you can spot any flawed assumption in its reasoning. For example, for a tricky business decision, it might list criteria and weigh options before recommending one.
事實上，在問題中加入像「讓我們一步一步來思考」這樣的短語，可以顯著提升在複雜推理任務上的準確性。你會因此看到 AI 為何會這樣回答，並能發現其推理中任何錯誤的假設。例如，對於一個困難的商業決策，它可能會先列出準則，再權衡各選項，最後才推薦一個方案。
    

    

      Self-Critique and Refinement
自我批判與修訂 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Provide your answer to [the task]. Then, critique your own answer – identify any weaknesses or mistakes. Finally, revise the answer to address the issues you found, and present the improved solution.”
提示：「提供你對[任務]的回答。然後，批判自己的回答 – 識別任何弱點或錯誤。最後，修訂回答以解決你發現的問題，並呈現改進後的解決方案。」
    

    

      Technique
      : This has the AI first answer, then switch roles to critic/reviewer of its own output, and then improve it. It’s a form of iterative refinement done in one prompt.
技巧：這讓 AI 先回答問題，再轉換角色為自身輸出的評論者或審閱者，最後再加以改善。這是一種在單一提示中完成的迭代修訂方式。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A higher-quality result. The initial answer is given, then the AI analyzes that answer critically (often finding subtle points to improve), and produces a second, refined answer. You effectively get the benefit of a review cycle without needing a second user prompt. For instance, if the task was to write an argument, the AI might first write it, then critique that it lacked examples, then add those in the final version. This yields a more polished outcome than a single-pass answer.
結果：獲得更高品質的結果。AI 會先提供初步回答，再對該回答進行嚴謹的分析（常常發現一些細微的改進點），並產生一個改進後的第二版回答。你實際上可以不用第二個使用者提示，就獲得評閱週期的效益。例如，如果任務是寫一篇論點文，AI 可能會先寫出論點，再評論指出缺乏範例，最後在最終版本中加入這些範例。這會比單一通回答出更精緻的結果。
    

    

      Constraint-Based Creativity
基於限制的創造力 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Generate [creative output] about [topic] with these constraints: [list your constraints]. (e.g. ‘Use exactly 50 words’, ‘Do not use the letter E’, ‘Incorporate the words: red, dawn, and whisper’.)”
提示：「根據這些限制生成 [創意產出] 關於 [主題]：[列出你的限制]。（例如：「使用正好 50 個字」、「不使用字母 E」、「包含這些詞彙：紅色、黎明、低語」）」
    

    

      Technique
      : Imposes artificial constraints or rules on the task to spur creative problem-solving. This can be stylistic (word count, vocabulary limits, rhyme scheme) or content-based.
技巧：在任務上施加人工限制或規則，以激發創意問題解決的過程。這些限制可以是風格上的（如字數限制、詞彙限制、押韻方式），也可以是內容上的。
    

    

      Outcome
      : The AI produces an answer that satisfies the constraints, often resulting in creative and novel formulations. For example, asking for a summary in exactly 50 words forces the answer to be very concise and focused. Or a story without the letter “E” (a lipogram) pushes the model to find alternate vocabulary – a challenging but interesting result. Constraint prompts ensure the output meets specific requirements (format, length, style) and encourage the model to think beyond the obvious. The results are tangible: you get content that fits your exact needs or creative outputs that follow unconventional rules.
結果：AI 會產生符合限制的答案，往往導致創意且獨特的表達方式。例如，要求用正好 50 個字來做摘要，會迫使答案非常簡潔且集中。又如要求寫一個不包含字母「E」的故事（一種稱為 lipogram 的寫作技巧），會促使模型尋找替代詞彙，這是一種具有挑戰性但有趣的結果。限制提示確保輸出符合特定要求（格式、長度、風格），並鼓勵模型思考超出常規的解決方案。結果是具體可見的：你會得到符合你精準需求的內容，或遵循非常規規則的創意產出。
    

    

      Business Strategy and Operations
商業策略與運營 
    

    

      This section’s prompts are geared toward business use cases, from high-level strategy formulation to operational planning and management tasks. 
本節的提示主要針對商業應用場景，從高層策略制定到運營規劃與管理任務皆有涵蓋。
    

    

      These prompts are designed to yield actionable plans, analyses, and decision-making support. They often leverage role-playing as business experts, structured frameworks, and multi-step reasoning to produce tangible business results.
這些提示旨在產生可執行的計畫、分析及決策支援。它們通常透過扮演商業專家、使用結構化框架及多步驟推理來達成具體的商業成果。
    

    

      Business Plan Generator
商業計畫產生器
    

    

      Prompt
      : “You are a startup consultant. Draft a comprehensive business plan for my new venture [brief description of business idea]. Include an Executive Summary, Market Analysis, Product/Service description, Business Model, Marketing & Sales strategy, and Financial projections. Each section should be a few paragraphs with relevant details.”
你是一位創業顧問。為我的新創業案[創業點子簡要描述]擬一份完整的商業計畫書。包含執行摘要、市場分析、產品/服務說明、商業模式、行銷與銷售策略，以及財務預測。每個部分應有幾段，並包含相關細節。
    

    

      Technique
      : Role-playing as a business consultant and explicitly listing plan sections (structure-based prompt).
技巧：以創業顧問身分進行角色扮演，並明確列出計畫書的各個部分（結構化提示）。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A structured business plan covering all key areas. The response will be organized into the requested sections, providing tangible content like market insights, monetization ideas, marketing approaches, and basic financial reasoning. This is far more useful than a generic one-paragraph answer—it reads like a real plan draft you can further refine.
結果：一份涵蓋所有關鍵領域的結構化商業計畫書。回應將依照所要求的各個部分進行組織，提供具體內容，例如市場洞察、營收模式、行銷方法以及基本財務分析。這比一般的單一段落回應更有用——它讀起來就像一份真實的計畫書草案，可以進一步修訂。 
    

    

      SWOT Analysis
SWOT 分析
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Perform a SWOT analysis for [Company or Product] in the [Industry] space. Outline 3-4 key Strengths, Weaknesses, Opportunities, and Threats. Make sure the points are specific to [the context of the company/product] and insightful (not generic).”
Prompt : 「為[公司或產品]在[產業]領域進行 SWOT 分析。列出 3-4 個關鍵的優勢、劣勢、機會與威脅。確保這些點與[公司或產品的背景]相關且具洞察力（非一般化）。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt using a well-known business framework (SWOT) to structure the answer.
Technique : 直接使用知名商業框架（SWOT）來結構回答。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A clear SWOT matrix with bullet points under each category (Strengths, Weaknesses, Opportunities, Threats). This provides tangible strategic insights – e.g.; strengths might highlight a strong distribution network, opportunities might point out a growing market segment to target, etc. You can directly use these points in strategy discussions or presentations.
Outcome : 一個清晰的 SWOT 矩陣，每個類別（優勢、劣勢、機會、威脅）下列出項目符號。這提供具體的戰略洞察 – 例如：優勢可能強調強大的通路網絡，機會可能指出可目標的成長市場區段等。這些點可以直接用於策略討論或簡報中。
    

    

      Defining OKRs (Objectives and Key Results)
定義 OKRs（目標與關鍵結果）
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Act as an OKR expert. Develop three high-level Objectives and 3 Key Results for each for our [team or project] focusing on [goal or strategy, e.g., improving customer satisfaction or increasing market share]. Make sure Objectives are qualitative and inspiring, and KRs are measurable targets with specific numbers or deliverables.”
扮演一個 OKR 專家。為我們的[團隊或專案]制定三個高階目標，並為每個目標制定三個關鍵結果，專注於[目標或策略，例如：提升客戶滿意度或增加市場佔有率]。請確保目標是質性且鼓舞人心的，而關鍵結果是可衡量的目標，包含具體的數字或成果。
    

    

      Technique
      : Role as an OKR coach plus a structured request (3 Objectives, each with 3 KRs) – a constraint that ensures a concrete output.
技巧：以 OKR 教練的角色加上結構化請求（3 個目標，每個目標有 3 個關鍵結果）——這是一種限制，確保輸出具體且實質。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A set of Objectives (e.g., “Enhance Customer Experience”), each followed by 3 Key Results (e.g., “Achieve NPS score of 60 by Q4”, “Reduce average support ticket resolution time to 4 hours”, etc.). You can practically copy-paste these tangible outcomes into your team’s OKR document. It turns an abstract goal into clear targets.
成果：一組目標（例如：「提升客戶體驗」），每個目標後面跟著三個關鍵結果（例如：「於 Q4 達成 NPS 分數 60」、「將平均客服單據處理時間縮短至 4 小時」等）。你可以直接將這些具體成果複製貼上到你們團隊的 OKR 文件中。它將抽象的目標轉化為明確的目標。
    

    

      Strategic Brainstorm – Multiple Growth Strategies
策略腦力激盪 – 多種成長策略
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our company wants to grow [metric or area, e.g., revenue or user base] next year. Generate five innovative growth strategies, each with a short explanation. Then briefly evaluate each strategy in terms of potential impact and feasibility.”
我們公司希望明年在[指標或領域，例如收入或用戶數量]上成長。請產生五種創新成長策略，每種策略附上簡短說明。然後針對每種策略，簡要評估其潛在影響力與可行性。
    

    

      Technique
      : It asks for multiple options (five strategies) plus a brief analysis of each (impact and feasibility)—essentially prompting brainstorming and evaluation.
技巧：它要求多種選擇（五種策略）加上每種策略的簡要分析（影響力與可行性）——基本上是在引導大腦風暴與評估。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A list of 5 distinct strategy ideas, for example, 1) Launching a referral program, 2) Expanding to a new market segment, 3) Upselling new features to existing customers, etc., each followed by an explanation. The added evaluation will give a sentence or two like “High impact as it leverages existing customers, feasibility is medium – requires developing a referral tracking system.” This prompt yields actionable choices and a quick SWOT for each idea, helping decide which growth path to pursue.
結果：列出五種不同的策略想法，例如：1) 啟動推薦計畫，2) 擴展至新的市場區段，3) 向現有客戶推廣新功能等，每種策略後附說明。附加的評估會提供一兩句評論，如「高影響力，因利用現有客戶，可行性中等 – 需要建立推薦追蹤系統。」此提示能產生具行動力的選擇，並為每個想法快速進行 SWOT 分析，幫助決定要採取哪條成長路線。
    

    

      Competitor Analysis
競爭對手分析
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We want to understand how we stack against [Competitor Name]. Compare our company to [Competitor] regarding product features, pricing, target market, and competitive advantages or disadvantages. Then suggest two strategic moves for us to gain an edge based on this comparison.”
我們想要了解我們與[對手名稱]相比如何。請比較我們的公司與[對手]在產品功能、價格、目標市場以及競爭優勢或劣勢方面的差異。然後根據此比較，提出兩個戰略行動，以幫助我們取得優勢。
    

    

      Technique
      : A direct analysis request, potentially invoking any knowledge the model has about the competitor (or the user can supply details). It ends with a request for strategic recommendations derived from the analysis.
技巧：這是一種直接的分析請求，可能會啟動模型對對手的任何相關知識（或用戶可提供詳細資訊）。最後會要求根據分析提出戰略建議。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A mini competitor analysis report. The AI will likely produce a paragraph or bullet points comparing key aspects: e.g., “Competitor has broader features in X, but we have better pricing; Competitor targets enterprise while we target small biz,” etc. This is followed by specific strategic suggestions such as “Focus on niche features that [Competitor] lacks,” or “Initiate a marketing campaign highlighting our lower cost,” etc. The result is actionable intelligence on your competitive positioning and ideas to improve it – a tangible benefit for strategic planning.
結果：一份簡短的競爭對手分析報告。AI 很可能會產生一段文字或項目符號來比較關鍵方面，例如：「對手在 X 方面有更廣泛的功能，但我們的價格更優；對手針對企業市場，而我們則針對小型企業。」等等。這之後會跟著具體的戰略建議，例如：「專注於對手缺乏的專業功能，」或「啟動一個強調我們較低成本的行銷活動，」等等。這項結果提供了關於競爭地位的可操作資訊，並提供改善的建議，對戰略規劃來說是一種實質的幫助。
    

    

      Recommended Model
      : GPT-4, especially if [Competitor Name] is a known entity – GPT-4’s training data can provide fairly detailed insight (up to 2021 knowledge). It will also be cautious and analytical rather than just copying marketing speak. GPT-3.5 can do this, too, but it might be more general (“Competitor is larger, we are smaller”) unless you feed it specifics. If you provide some data about both companies, GPT-3.5 can work with that. Claude is helpful if you have a lot of text (e.g., excerpts from websites or reviews for both your company and the competitor) – Claude can ingest those and produce a synthesis due to their context length, making the analysis very evidence-based. Be mindful that any model’s knowledge might be outdated – if the competitor changed something recently, the AI might not know. You can always correct or provide updated info in the prompt. Gemini could cross-reference various modalities (perhaps analyzing a competitor’s website screenshot or data table in the future) to enrich the comparison. In short, for analysis depth: GPT-4 or Claude. For quick baseline: GPT-3.5.
建議模型 : GPT-4，特別是當[對手名稱]為已知的實體時 – GPT-4 的訓練資料可以提供相當詳細的洞察（知識更新至 2021 年）。它也會更加謹慎且分析性，而不是只是複製行銷用語。GPT-3.5 也可以做到，但可能會比較一般化（「對手較大，我們較小」）除非你提供具體資訊。如果你提供兩家公司的一些資料，GPT-3.5 也能處理。如果擁有大量文字（例如你公司與對手的網站摘錄或評論），Claude 會很有幫助 – Claude 可以吸收這些資料並產生綜合分析，因為其上下文長度較長，使分析更具證據基礎。請注意任何模型的知識都可能過時 – 如果對手最近有變動，AI 可能不知道。你總是可以透過提示語進行修正或提供更新的資訊。Gemini 未來或許可以跨參考不同類型的資料（例如分析對手網站的截圖或資料表），以豐富比較內容。總而言之，對於分析深度：建議使用 GPT-4 或 Claude。對於快速基準分析：GPT-3.5 即可。
    

    

      Decision Matrix (Pros, Cons, Recommendation)
決策矩陣（優點、缺點、建議）
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We are debating between Option A and B for [business decision context]. Please compare the two options: list the key pros and cons in a table or a clear format. Then give a recommendation on which to choose and why, considering factors like cost, risk, and long-term benefit.”
我們正在討論在[業務決策情境]中選擇 Option A 或 B。請比較這兩個選項：以表格或清晰的格式列出各自的優點與缺點。然後根據成本、風險和長期效益等因素，給出一個推薦意見，說明為何選擇某個選項。
    

    

      Technique
      : This uses a comparison framework (pros/cons) and requests a recommendation, effectively guiding the model through a fundamental decision analysis.
技巧：這使用了比較框架（優點/缺點）並要求推薦，有效地引導模型進行基本的決策分析。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A side-by-side comparison of Option A vs Option B, which might be formatted as two columns (if the model outputs a markdown table or bullet list for each). For example, if A = outsource a task and B = build in-house, it will list the Pros/Cons for each option. Following that, a clear recommendation section, e.g., “Recommendation: Go with Option A because ... (some rationale).” This output directly supports decision-making, giving you a tangible analysis document rather than just an opinion. You can easily show this to stakeholders or use it to double-check your thinking.
結果：Option A 與 Option B 的並列比較，可能以兩欄的格式呈現（如果模型輸出為 markdown 表格或每個選項的項目清單）。例如，若 A 為外包任務，B 為內建團隊，則會列出每個選項的優缺點。接下來是明確的推薦部分，例如：「推薦：選擇 Option A，因為...（某些理由）。」此輸出直接支持決策，提供您一個具體的分析文件，而非僅是意見。您可以輕易地向利害關係人展示，或用來重新檢視自己的想法。
    

    

      Risk Assessment and Mitigation Plan
風險評估與緩解計畫
    

    

      Prompt
      : “For our upcoming [project/initiative], identify the top 5 risks that could impact success. For each risk, assess its likelihood (High/Med/Low) and impact (High/Med/Low), and then propose a mitigation strategy. Present the results in a clear list or table.”
我們即將啟動的[專案/計畫]，請識別可能影響成功的前五大風險。針對每個風險，評估其發生機率（高/中/低）與影響程度（高/中/低），並提出緩衝策略。以清晰的清單或表格呈現結果。
    

    

      Technique
      : Structured prompt focusing on risk management: identify -> assess -> mitigate. This ensures the output isn’t just a list of risks; each is analyzed and addressed.
技巧：結構化提示，專注於風險管理：識別 → 評估 → 緩衝。這確保輸出不只是風險清單，每個風險都會被分析並提出對應的解決方案。
    

    

      Outcome: A practical risk register. You’ll get something like:
結果：一個實用的風險登記冊。您將得到類似以下的內容：
    

    

      Risk: X (Likelihood: High, Impact: Low) – Mitigation: do Y.
風險：X（發生機率：高，影響程度：低） – 緩衝策略：做 Y。
    

    

      Risk: ... and so on.
風險：... 以及如此類推。
    

    

      For example, “Risk: Supplier delay – Likelihood: Medium, Impact: High – Mitigation: maintain backup supplier or stock critical components.” This output is directly usable for project planning. You have tangible items to monitor and action plans in place.
例如，「風險：供應商延遲 – 可能性：中等，影響：高 – 緩衝措施：維持備用供應商或儲備關鍵零件。」此輸出可以直接用於專案規劃。你有具體的項目可以監控，並已制定行動計畫。
    

    

      Change Management Plan
變革管理計畫
    

    

      Prompt
      : “You are an expert in organizational change. Outline a change management plan for a company implementing [describe change, e.g., a new software system or a process change]. Include steps to prepare for the change, how to communicate it to employees, training or support needed, and methods to handle resistance. Present it as a brief step-by-step guide.”
提示：「你是一位組織變革專家。請為一家正在實施[描述變革，例如新軟體系統或流程變革]的公司，制定一份變革管理計畫。包含準備變革的步驟、如何與員工溝通、需要的培訓或支援，以及處理抵觸的方法。請以簡潔的逐步指南形式呈現。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role-playing as a change management consultant and requesting a step-by-step plan with specific subtopics (communication, training, resistance).
技巧 : 以變革管理顧問身分進行角色扮演，並要求提供一個逐步進行的計畫，包含具體子主題（溝通、培訓、抵觸）。 
    

    

      Outcome
      : A concise change management strategy. Likely formatted in steps: e.g., Step 1: Define the vision and urgency (with an explanation), Step 2: Stakeholder alignment, Step 3: Communication plan (what, when, how), Step 4: Training sessions scheduling, Step 5: Feedback channels and addressing pushback, etc. This is directly actionable – it reads like an implementation checklist for the change. Managers could use it to ensure they cover all bases during the transition.
成果 : 一個簡明的變革管理策略。通常會以步驟形式呈現，例如：步驟 1：定義願景與緊迫感（附說明），步驟 2：利害相關者對齊，步驟 3：溝通計畫（內容、時間、方式），步驟 4：培訓課程排程，步驟 5：反饋管道與處理抵觸，等等。這是一份可以直接執行的計畫 – 看起來就像是變革實踐的檢查清單。經理人可以利用它來確保在轉變過程中覆蓋所有重要環節。 
    

    

      Socratic Strategy Coach
蘇格拉底策略教練 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Let’s do a strategy exercise. Act as a veteran CEO coach. I will outline my business’s situation and challenges, and you will ask me three probing questions to diagnose the key issues. I will answer them (imagining likely responses), and then you will provide a tailored strategic advice plan based on that information.”
提示 : 「我們來做一個策略練習。請你以資深 CEO 教練的身分來扮演。我會說明我公司的狀況與挑戰，而你則要提出三個深入的問題來診斷關鍵問題。我會回答這些問題（假設可能的回答），然後你根據這些資訊提供一個針對性的策略建議計畫。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role-playing combined with a multi-turn Socratic approach. The prompt explicitly instructs the AI to ask questions, wait (in practice, you’d answer), and give advice.
技巧：角色扮演結合多回合的蘇格拉底式提問法。提示明確指示 AI 進行提問、等待（實際上是您回答），並給予建議。
    

    

      Outcome
      : This prompt initiates an interactive consultation session. In practice, the AI will output three thoughtful questions like an honest consultant would (“What does your current sales process look like?”, “What do you see as your biggest operational bottleneck?” etc.). As the user, you can either answer those in the chat or, as the prompt suggests, have the AI assume likely answers to proceed (if you’re using this as a one-shot demonstration). Ultimately, the outcome is a strategic advice plan tailored to the specifics discussed. This is powerful because the advice is not generic – it’s shaped by the Q&A, ensuring tangible relevance. The format guides you (or the AI acting as you) to think critically about the business before jumping to solutions.
結果：這個提示會啟動一個互動式的諮詢會話。實際上，AI 會輸出三個深入的問題，就像誠實的顧問一樣（例如：「您目前的銷售流程是什麼樣子？」、「您認為最大的運營瓶頸是什麼？」等）。作為使用者，您可以選擇在聊天中回答這些問題，或如提示所建議的，讓 AI 假設可能的答案以繼續進行（如果您是用這個作為一次性的示範）。最終的結果是根據討論內容而量身打造的策略建議計畫。這一點非常強大，因為建議不是泛泛而談的，而是透過問答來塑造，確保具體且相關。這個格式會引導您（或 AI 代表您）在跳入解決方案之前，進行深入的思考。 
    

    

      Industry Trends Report
產業趨勢報告
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Generate a brief industry trends report for the [industry name] industry. Identify 3-5 current major trends or challenges in this industry and describe each. Then, for a company in this space (like ours), suggest a strategic recommendation to capitalize on or address each trend.”
生成一份[產業名稱]產業的簡要產業趨勢報告。識別此產業目前的 3-5 個主要趨勢或挑戰，並分別描述。然後，為該產業中的公司（例如我們的公司）提出一個戰略建議，以利用或應對每個趨勢。
    

    

      Technique: Direct request for analysis of an industry with a two-part output: listing trends and making recommendations.
技巧：直接要求對產業進行分析，產生兩部分輸出：列出趨勢並提出建議。
    

    

      Outcome: A mini-industry analysis document. For example, if the industry is electric vehicles, Trend 1 might be “Increasing battery efficiency,” described with a sentence or two, and the recommendation might be “Invest in R&D for next-gen batteries or partner with battery tech firms.” You get a broad view by listing multiple trends (3-5). This is tangible competitive intelligence – you could use it in planning sessions or as talking points in a strategy meeting. It turns broad market research into concrete suggestions for your company.
成果：一份小型產業分析文件。例如，若產業是電動車，趨勢 1 可能是「電池效率提升」，用一兩句描述，建議可能是「投資下一代電池的研發或與電池技術公司合作」。透過列出多個趨勢（3-5 個），你可獲得廣泛的視野。這是一種具體的競爭情報，可以用於規劃會議或作為策略會議的談話重點。它將廣泛的市場研究轉化為對你公司的具體建議。 
    

    

      Process Improvement (Lean Analysis)
流程改善（Lean 分析）
    

    

      Prompt
      : “I will describe our current process for [task, e.g., order fulfillment]. Identify three inefficiencies or pain points in this process, and for each, suggest a specific improvement or solution (think Lean methodology). Make the suggestions practical (e.g., eliminate a step, automate something, clarify a role, etc.).”
提示：「我將描述我們目前的[任務，例如：訂單處理]流程。請辨識此流程中的三個低效率或痛點，並為每個痛點提出一個具體的改進或解決方案（思考 Lean 方法論）。讓建議變得實際可行（例如：消除一個步驟、自動化某個流程、明確一個角色等）。」
    

    

      Technique: Asks the AI to perform a process analysis, find inefficiencies, -> suggest improvements. This is enhanced by providing context (the user would insert a process description; the prompt indicates you will give it).
技巧：要求 AI 進行流程分析，找出低效率的地方，並提出改進建議。這會因提供情境（用戶會插入流程描述；提示表示你將提供）而得到加強。
    

    

      Outcome: A set of pinpointed process improvements. For example: “Pain Point: Redundant data entry in step 3 – Improvement: Implement an integrated software to auto-transfer data from system A to B, removing the manual re-entry.” With three such recommendations, you have tangible changes to consider to make your operation more efficient. This is essentially getting consultative advice on process optimization.
結果：一組具體的流程改進建議。例如：「痛點：步驟 3 中重複的資料輸入 – 改進：實行整合軟體，自動從系統 A 轉移資料至系統 B，去除手動重新輸入的步驟。」透過三個這樣的建議，你會有具體的變革可以考慮，以提升作業效率。這基本上是在獲得關於流程最佳化的諮詢建議。
    

    

      Meeting Agenda & Summary Draft
會議議程與摘要草案
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We have a meeting about [topic]. Draft an agenda with 4-5 bullet points (topics to cover) and allocate a rough time for each (for a 1-hour meeting). Also, draft a follow-up email summarizing the meeting’s key decisions and action items (you can invent plausible outcomes for the draft). The tone should be professional and clear.”
我們有一個關於[主題]的會議，請草擬一個包含 4-5 個重點事項的議程，並為每個事項分配一個大約的時間（會議總長為一小時）。同時，也請草擬一封後續電子郵件，總結會議中的主要決議與待辦事項（您可以假設合理的結果作為草案）。語氣應專業且清晰。
    

    

      Technique
      : This technique combines two related tasks—creating a structured agenda and a summary email—in one prompt, showing multi-step content generation. We even allow the AI to assume plausible outcomes for demonstration.
技巧：這個技巧結合了兩個相關任務—建立結構化的議程與總結電子郵件—於一個提示中，展現多步驟的內容生成。我們甚至允許 AI 假設合理的結果以進行示範。
    

    

      Outcome
      : Two concrete pieces of content: 1) Meeting agenda – e.g., “1. Introduction (5 min), 2. Budget Review (15 min), 3. Project Updates (30 min), 4. Next Steps (10 min)”. 2) Follow-up email – with a header like “Subject: Summary of [Meeting]” and a body that states decisions (e.g., “decided to increase Q2 marketing budget by 10%”) and lists action items (“Alice will prepare the budget update by Monday”). These outputs save time for any manager – you get a ready-to-use agenda to distribute before the meeting and a summary draft to send after. Even though the AI invented outcomes, you would replace those with actual ones after the meeting; the template is what matters.
成果 : 兩個具體的內容：1) 會議議程 – 例如：「1. 開場說明 (5 分鐘), 2. 預算審查 (15 分鐘), 3. 專案進度 (30 分鐘), 4. 下一步行動 (10 分鐘)」。2) 後續郵件 – 以「主旨：[會議] 總結」為標題，內容說明決議事項（例如：「決定將第二季行銷預算提高 10%」）並列出待辦事項（例如：「Alice 將於週一準備預算更新」）。這些輸出可節省任何經理的時間 – 你會得到一個可以直接使用的議程，用來在會議前發送給與會者，以及一個總結草案，用來在會議後發送。雖然 AI 產生了這些成果，但實際上你會在會議後替換為真實的內容；模板才是重點。
    

    

      Policy Drafting
政策擬訂 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our company needs a new policy on [topic] (for example, a Remote Work Policy). Draft a concise policy that includes Purpose, Scope (who it applies to), Policy Guidelines (the rules or expectations), and Consequences for non-compliance (if relevant). Use clear bullet points or sub-sections for readability. The tone should be formal but positive.”
提示 : 「我們公司需要針對 [主題] 設定新的政策（例如：遠端工作政策）。請擬訂一個簡潔的政策，包含目的、適用範圍（針對誰）、政策準則（規則或預期行為）以及不遵守的後果（如有相關）。為提高可讀性，請使用明確的項目符號或子節。語氣應正式但正面。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct content generation with a specified structure for the policy and desired tone. This guides the AI in producing an organized document.
技巧：以指定的結構直接產生內容，並設定期望的語氣。這會引導 AI 產生一個有條理的文件。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A draft company policy document. It will come out structured into sections as requested. For a Remote Work Policy example, you’d get sections like Purpose (why the policy exists), Scope (e.g., “All full-time employees”), Guidelines (bullet points like “Employees must be online between 10 am-4 pm” etc.), and Consequences (e.g., “Repeated violation may result in review by HR”). This is a tangible result – a nearly ready-to-use policy that you can then tweak to fit exact company requirements. It saves a ton of time starting from scratch.
成果：一份公司政策草案。它會依照要求的結構分為各個部分。例如，針對遠端工作政策，您會得到如目的（為何需要此政策）、範圍（例如「所有全職員工」）、指引（如「員工必須在上午 10 點至下午 4 點之間在線」等項目符號）、後果（例如「重複違規可能導致人資部審查」）等部分。這是一份可見的成果——一份幾乎可以直接使用的政策文件，您可以再根據公司的實際需求進行調整。這能節省大量從零開始的時間。
    

    

      Training Session Outline
訓練課程大綱 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “You are a training specialist. Design an outline for a training workshop on [topic] for [target audience, e.g., new managers or sales team]. Include the learning objectives (what trainees should learn), a list of key topics/modules to cover (with short descriptions), and one interactive activity or discussion idea to engage participants. Format the output as a clear outline.”
提示：「你是一位訓練專員。請為[主題]的訓練工作坊設計一個大綱，針對[目標受訓對象，例如新任主管或銷售團隊]。包含學習目標（受訓者應學習的內容）、需涵蓋的關鍵主題/模組清單（附短描述），以及一個互動活動或討論點以吸引參與者。請以清晰的大綱格式呈現。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role as a training specialist with a request for an outline structure (objectives, topics, activity). This ensures the result is organized and actionable.
技巧 : 請以訓練專員身分，提出一個課程大綱結構（目標、主題、活動）。這能確保結果有條理且具可操作性。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A training workshop outline. For example, for new managers, Objectives might be “Understand effective feedback techniques; Learn time management for team projects; etc.” Topics could be numbered: 1. Transitioning to Management (description...), 2. Communication & Feedback (description...), 3. Delegation Skills, etc. Each with a sentence on content. And an interactive activity like “Role-play a difficult conversation and debrief.” This output gives you a tangible framework for a training session that you can expand into slides or a lesson plan. It’s high-impact because it provides the scaffold for educating your team.
成果 : 一個訓練工作坊的大綱。例如，針對新任主管，目標可能是「了解有效的回饋技巧；學習團隊專案的時間管理；等等。」主題可以編號：1. 轉換為主管（說明...），2. 沟通與回饋（說明...），3. 委派技巧，等等。每個主題附上一句內容說明。並搭配互動活動，例如「角色扮演困難對話並進行回饋討論。」這個輸出提供你一個具體的框架，可以用來擴展成簡報或課程計畫。它具有高影響力，因為它為教育團隊提供了基礎架構。
    

    

      Performance Review Feedback
績效評核回饋
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Act as a manager. Write a performance review paragraph for an employee who [describe performance scenario] – e.g., met their sales targets, collaborates well with the team, but needs to improve time management. The feedback should be constructive and balanced, highlighting specific accomplishments and one or two areas for improvement, in a supportive tone.”
提示 : 「請以主管身分，為一位員工寫一段績效評核內容，例如：達成銷售目標、與團隊合作良好，但需要改善時間管理。回饋應具建設性且平衡，強調具體的成績與一到兩個改進領域，並以支持性的語氣呈現。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role-play as a manager giving feedback, with a specific scenario provided to ground the content. Emphasizes a balanced approach (positive + improvement).
技巧 : 以經理身分進行角色扮演，給予回饋，並提供特定情境以作為內容的基礎。強調平衡的作法（正面 + 改進點）。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A well-crafted performance review paragraph or two. For the example given, the output might say: “Jane has consistently met her sales targets for Q3, even exceeding them by 10%, and teammates often praise her for her willingness to share knowledge and assist on group projects. Her client relations skills are a strong asset to the team. One area to develop further is her time management – ensuring deadlines for submitting reports. By focusing on better prioritization, Jane can become even more effective. Overall, she’s a valuable team member who positively impacts team morale.” This kind of output is directly usable in a performance appraisal document. It’s tangible and saves a manager considerable time formulating feedback from scratch.
成果 : 一個精心撰寫的績效評估段落或兩段。例如，輸出可能是：「Jane 在第三季 consistently 達成銷售目標，甚至超出 10%，且隊友常讚揚她樂於分享知識並協助團隊專案。她的客戶關係技巧是團隊的重要資產。一個可以進一步提升的領域是時間管理 – 確保報告提交的期限。透過更有效的優先順序安排，Jane 可以變得更加高效。總體而言，她是團隊中寶貴的一員，對團隊士氣有正面影響。」這種輸出可以直接應用在績效評估文件中。它具體且實用，節省經理從頭撰寫回饋的大量時間。
    

    

      Customer Complaint Response (Email)
客戶投訴回應（電子郵件）
    

    

      Prompt
      : “You are a customer support agent. Write an email response to a customer complaint about [issue]. The customer is upset because [summarize complaint: e.g., they received a faulty product and haven’t gotten a replacement]. Apologize sincerely, address their concern, and offer a solution (refund, replacement, discount, etc.). Keep the tone empathetic, polite, and reassuring.”
提示：「你是一名客服代理。請寫一封回覆客戶投訴的電子郵件。客戶對[問題]感到不滿，他們因為[總結投訴內容：例如，他們收到有瑕疵的商品且尚未收到替代品]而感到生氣。請誠摯道歉，處理他們的問題，並提供解決方案（如退款、更換商品、折扣等）。保持語氣同理、禮貌且令人安心。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role-play as a support agent using a specific customer scenario. Instructs inclusion of key elements: apology, addressing issue, offering solution.
技巧：透過角色扮演作為客服代理，使用特定的客戶情境。指示包含關鍵要素：道歉、處理問題、提供解決方案。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A professional customer service email that likely starts with an apology, acknowledges the issue, provides a resolution, and ends on a positive/helpful note. For example: “Dear [Customer Name], I’m truly sorry to hear that the product you received was faulty... We take full responsibility... As a solution, I’ve arranged for a free replacement to be shipped immediately... I understand your frustration and appreciate your patience... Please let me know if there’s anything else... etc.” This kind of response can directly be used (with slight tweaks like order numbers). It’s tangible because it addresses the customer’s problem and hopefully restores goodwill.
成果 : 一封專業的客服郵件，通常以道歉為開頭，承認問題，提供解決方案，並以正面或有幫助的語氣作結。例如：「親愛的[客戶姓名]，聽到您收到的商品有瑕疵，我感到非常抱歉... 我們對此負全責... 作為解決方案，我已安排免費更換商品立即發送... 我明白您的不滿，也感謝您的耐心... 請問還有其他需要協助的地方嗎... 等等。」這種回應可以直接使用（只需稍作調整，如訂單編號）。這是具體的，因為它解決了客戶的問題，並希望能恢復客戶的滿意度。
    

    

      Negotiation Strategy Brief
談判策略簡述 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “I’m preparing to negotiate a deal with [who/what]. Outline a negotiation strategy for me. Include my goal in the negotiation, the other party’s likely interests, three key points or offers I should emphasize, and potential compromises or BATNA (best alternative if we don’t reach a deal). Also, suggest one or two tough questions the other side might ask and how I could respond.”
提示 : 「我即將與[誰/什麼]進行談判。請為我擬定一個談判策略。包括我在談判中的目標、對方可能的立場、我應該強調的三個重點或提議、以及可能的妥協方案或 BATNA（若談判不成的最佳替代方案）。另外，請建議一個或兩個對方可能會提出的困難問題，以及我該如何回答。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Ask for a structured negotiation plan, including BATNA (an advanced concept) and even a bit of role-play by prepping for tough questions.
技巧 : 要求一個結構化的談判計畫，包含 BATNA（一個高階概念）以及一些角色扮演，預備應對困難的問題。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A negotiation briefing. For example, if negotiating a supplier contract: Goal – “secure 15% discount while establishing long-term relationship”, Other party’s interests – “keep pricing profitable, secure a long-term client,” Key points – “our volume of orders, willingness to sign longer contract, our strategic alignment,” Potential compromises – “settle for 10% discount but with faster payment terms (if 15% not possible), or consider a shorter contract as BATNA to test other suppliers”. The tricky question might be, “Why should we give you a discount when our prices are already competitive?” with a suggested answer. This is very actionable – like notes you’d take into a negotiation meeting.
成果 : 談判簡報。例如，若在談判供應商合約：目標 – 「取得 15%折扣同時建立長期合作關係」，對方的興趣 – 「維持價格有競爭力，獲得長期客戶」，重點 – 「我們的訂單量、願意簽訂較長合約、我們的策略契合度」，可能的妥協點 – 「若無法取得 15%折扣，則接受 10%折扣但換取更快的付款條件，或考慮以較短合約作為 BATNA 來測試其他供應商」。困難的問題可能是：「為何我們要給你們折扣，當我們的價格已經很有競爭力了？」並附上建議回答。這非常具操作性，就像你會帶進談判會議的筆記。
    

    

      Press Release Draft
新聞稿草案
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our company is announcing [news/event] (e.g., a new product launch or a big partnership). Write a press release announcing this. It should have a catchy headline, a strong opening paragraph that covers the who/what/when/where/why, a quote from a company executive, and a closing that mentions where to find more information. Keep it to about 3–4 short paragraphs in a professional, newsy tone.”
促銷 : 「我們公司即將宣佈 [新聞/活動] （例如：新產品發佈或重大合作）。請撰寫一篇宣傳稿宣布此消息。內容應包含一個吸引人的標題、一個涵蓋誰、什麼、何時、何地、為何的強勢導語段落、一位公司高層的引述，以及結尾提及可尋找更多資訊的地方。請保持在 3 至 4 個簡短段落之間，語氣專業且具新聞性。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct content creation with a specific journalistic format (press release structure: headline, lead, quote, boilerplate/close).
技巧 : 以特定的新聞格式直接進行內容創作（宣傳稿結構：標題、導語、引述、公司簡介/結尾）。 
    

    

      Outcome
      : A ready-to-go press release. For example:
結果 : 一篇即用的宣傳稿。例如： 
    

    

      Headline:
       “XYZ Corp Unveils Innovative ABC Platform, Transforming Online Learning”
標題：「XYZ Corp 發佈創新 ABC 平台，革新線上學習」
    

    

      Lead paragraph:
       covering key facts about the launch.
導語段落：說明產品發佈的重點資訊。
    

    

      Quote:
       e.g., “We’re excited to...,” said John Doe, CEO.
引述：例如，John Doe，CEO 表示：「我們很興奮能...」。
    

    

      Closing:
       info about the company and contact details (maybe the model will include a generic boilerplate).
結尾：包含公司資訊與聯繫方式（可能模型會包含通用的結尾段落）。
    

    

      This is a highly tangible piece of writing – often, companies spend a while drafting press releases. The AI can produce a solid draft that you can then fine-tune with specifics.
這是一篇非常具體的寫作內容－通常，公司會花費一段時間來撰寫新聞稿。AI 可以產生一個扎實的初稿，之後你再根據具體細節進行調整。
    

    

      Metrics Analysis Brainstorm
指標分析大腦風暴 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our [metric] has changed significantly: [describe data, e.g., ‘website traffic dropped 20% last month’]. Brainstorm 3-4 possible reasons for this change, backing each with a plausible explanation or hypothesis. Then, for each reason, suggest one way to investigate or address it. (Assume we have limited info so that you can be creative but logical.)”
提示：「我們的[指標]有顯著的變化：[描述數據，例如：『網站流量上個月下降了 20%』]。請大腦風暴 3 到 4 個可能的變化原因，並為每個原因提供一個合理的解釋或假設。然後，針對每個原因，提出一個調查或處理的方法。(假設我們資訊有限，請發揮創意但保持邏輯性。)」
    

    

      Technique
      : Analytical prompt requesting diagnosis of a metric change plus an actionable follow-up for each hypothesis (investigate/mitigate).
技巧：分析性提示，要求診斷指標變化的問題，並為每個假設提出具體的後續行動方案（調查/緩解）。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A set of hypotheses for the metric change and corresponding next steps. For instance: “Reason 1: Seasonality – perhaps last month is historically slow (check Google Analytics year-over-year for same month). Reason 2: Recent website redesign might have affected SEO (investigate by checking keyword rankings or any drop in search traffic). 
結果：一個指標變化的假設集合及相應的下一步行動。例如：「原因 1：季節性因素 – 可能上個月是歷史上的淡季（可透過 Google Analytics 查看同月份的年對年數據）。原因 2：最近的網站重新設計可能影響了 SEO（可透過檢查關鍵字排名或搜索流量下降情況來進行調查）。」
    

    

      Reason 3
      : Competitor campaign – a competitor launched a big promotion drawing audience (address by launching our campaign or checking social media buzz).” This output is valuable for a team trying to diagnose a sudden change; it provides a starting checklist of things to look into, turning confusion into a plan of action.
理由 3：競爭對手的行銷活動 – 競爭對手發起了大型促銷活動，吸引顧客（例如透過啟動我們的行銷活動或查看社交媒體熱度）。此輸出對於團隊診斷突然的變化非常有價值；它提供了一個初步的檢查清單，將混亂轉化為具體的行動計畫。
    

    

      Ethical Dilemma Advice
倫理困境建議 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “You are an ethics compliance advisor. Our company faces an ethical dilemma: 
      [describe scenario]
       (e.g., we discovered a minor safety issue in our product that’s not legally required to be reported but could pose some risk). Analyze the situation regarding ethical obligations vs. business interests, then recommend what to do. The advice should reference relevant principles (like transparency, customer safety, long-term trust) and be pragmatic.”
提示：「你是一名倫理合規顧問。我們公司面臨一個倫理困境：[描述情境]（例如：我們發現產品中有一個小的安全問題，雖然不需依法報告，但可能帶來某些風險）。請分析此情境中倫理義務與商業利益的關係，並提出應採取的行動建議。建議應參考相關原則（如透明度、顧客安全、長期信任）且具實用性。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role as ethics advisor, scenario analysis, weighing principles, and giving a clear recommendation.
技巧：扮演倫理顧問角色、情境分析、權衡原則，並給予明確的建議。
    

    

      Outcome
      : An ethical decision analysis. The response will likely outline the considerations: for example, “Ethical Obligation: ensure customer safety and be transparent—aligns with values and long-term trust. Business Interest: avoid potential recall costs and PR fallout.” 
成果 : 一個倫理決策分析。回應可能會說明考量因素：例如，「倫理義務：確保客戶安全並保持透明—這與價值觀和長期信任一致。商業利益：避免潛在的產品回收成本與公共關係危機。」
    

    

      While not legally required to report, ethically, it’s advisable to inform users… Recommendation: Proactively disclose the issue and offer a fix or replacement, emphasizing your commitment to safety. 
雖然沒有法律義務要報告，但從倫理角度來看，建議告知用戶… 建議：主動揭露問題並提供解決方案或更換商品，強調對安全的承諾。
    

    

      This mitigates future liability and builds trust, even with short-term cost.” Such an output is valuable because it provides a reasoned perspective that might align with an ethics code or simply common sense, helping leaders make a choice that isn’t just about immediate profit but also reputation and integrity.
這可以降低未來的責任風險並建立信任，即使短期會有成本。」這樣的輸出是有價值的，因為它提供了一個有理有據的觀點，可能符合倫理準則或只是常識，幫助領導者做出不僅僅是關於即時利潤，也關於聲譽與誠信的選擇。
    

    

      Automation Opportunities
自動化機會
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We want to automate parts of our [process/business area]. I will describe our current workflow. Identify three tasks in this workflow that are good candidates for automation (e.g., repetitive, manual, time-consuming). For each task, suggest what type of tool or software could automate it (for instance, an Excel macro, a script, an RPA bot, a SaaS platform, etc.) and the potential benefit (time saved, error reduction, etc.).”
我們想要自動化我們的[流程/業務領域]中的一些部分。我將描述我們目前的作業流程。請辨識此流程中三個適合自動化的任務（例如：重複性、手動、耗時的任務）。針對每個任務，建議什麼類型的工具或軟體可以用來自動化它（例如：Excel 宏、腳本、RPA 機器人、SaaS 平台等），以及潛在的效益（節省時間、減少錯誤等）。
    

    

      Technique
      : Analytical prompt focusing on process automation. It requires understanding the workflow (provided by the user) and matching steps to automation solutions.
技巧：分析型提示，專注於流程自動化。此提示需要理解用戶提供的作業流程，並將步驟與自動化解決方案進行匹配。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A set of automation recommendations. For example, the output might say:
結果：一組自動化建議。例如，輸出可能如下：
    

    

      Task
      : “Data entry from form to system” – Candidate for automation via an RPA (Robotic Process Automation) bot or a simple integration script. Benefit: saves ~2 hours/day and eliminates copy-paste errors.
任務：「從表單輸入資料至系統」 – 可以透過 RPA（機器人流程自動化）機器人或簡單的整合腳本來自動化。效益：每天節省約 2 小時，並消除複製貼上的錯誤。
    

    

      Task
      : “Monthly report generation” – This could be automated with an Excel macro or BI tool that updates a dashboard. Benefit: frees up analyst’s time and provides real-time access to data.
任務 : 「月報生成」 – 可以透過 Excel 宏或 BI 工具自動更新看板來實現。好處是節省分析師的時間，並提供即時的數據存取。 
    

    

      Task
      : “Emailing order confirmations”—Use an email automation tool or script triggered by order completion. The benefit is quicker communication with customers and less manual sending.
任務 : 「發送訂單確認信」—使用電子郵件自動化工具或在訂單完成時觸發的腳本。好處是能更快地與客戶溝通，並減少手動發送的步驟。 
    

    

      These are tangible, actionable suggestions. A manager or IT person could explore those specific solutions. This essentially jumpstarts an automation initiative by highlighting low-hanging fruit.
這些是具體且可執行的建議。經理或 IT 人員可以探討這些特定的解決方案。這基本上透過指出容易實現的方案，啟動了一個自動化計畫。 
    

    

      Financial Model Assumptions
財務模型假設
    

    

      Prompt
      : “I’m building a financial model for a [type of business] (e.g., a subscription box service). List five key assumptions I should include in the model (such as customer growth rate, average revenue per customer, etc.), and each assumption provides a reasonable initial value or range and a one-sentence justification. Make sure these assumptions are relevant to this business model.”
提示：「我正在為一種[商業類型]（例如訂閱盒服務）建立財務模型。請列出五個我應該包含在模型中的關鍵假設（例如客戶成長率、每位客戶平均收入等），每個假設需提供一個合理的初始值或範圍，以及一句說明理由。請確保這些假設與此商業模式相關。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Focused prompt asking for core assumptions in a financial context, with rationale. This guides the AI in thinking of the drivers of a business model.
技巧：聚焦於財務情境中的核心假設，並附上理由。這會引導 AI 思考商業模式的驅動因素。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A set of key financial assumptions with values and reasoning. For a subscription box service, for example:
結果：一組關鍵財務假設，包含數值與說明理由。例如針對訂閱盒服務：
    

    

      Assumption
       
      1
      : Monthly Subscription Price—Initial value: $25 per box. Justification: Based on the market average for similar services, this covers product and shipping costs with a margin.
假設 1：每月訂閱價格—初始值：每盒 25 美元。說明：根據類似服務的市場平均價格，此價格可覆蓋產品與運送成本並有邊際利潤。
    

    

      Assumption 2
      : Subscriber Growth Rate—Initial value: 10% monthly for the first 6 months, tapering to 3% by year 2. Justification: High early growth due to marketing push, then slowing as the market saturates.
假設 2：用戶成長率—初始值：前 6 個月每月成長 10%，到第二年減至 3%。說明：由於行銷推廣，初期成長較快，之後市場趨近飽和，成長速度減緩。
    

    

      Assumption 3
      : Churn Rate—Value: 5% of subscribers cancel per month. Justification: This is typical for subscription services and ensures that not all customers stay indefinitely.
假設 3：用戶流失率—值：每月有 5%的訂閱用戶取消。說明：這在訂閱式服務中是常見的現象，並確保並非所有客戶都會無限期留存。
    

    

      Etc.
等等。
    

    

      This is very useful when setting up a model, as these assumptions become the inputs for calculations. The justification also helps explain to stakeholders why those numbers were chosen (and can be tweaked with reasoning).
這在建立模型時非常有用，因為這些假設會成為計算的輸入資料。說明也能幫助利害關係人了解為何選擇這些數字（並可根據理由進行調整）。
    

    

      Project Plan Outline
專案計畫大綱 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We need to execute [project name or goal] (e.g., launch a new e-commerce website) in the next 3 months. Outline a high-level project plan, including major phases or milestones (like Planning, Development, Testing, and Launch), and for each phase, list the key tasks or deliverables and an estimated timeline/duration. Present it in a structured format (for example, a list or table).”
提示 : 「我們需要在接下來的三個月內執行[專案名稱或目標]（例如，啟動一個新的電商網站）。請列出一個高階的專案計畫，包括主要階段或里程碑（如規劃、開發、測試和發佈），並為每個階段列出關鍵任務或成果，以及預估的時間線或持續時間。請以結構化格式呈現（例如清單或表格）。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt for a project plan outline with phases, tasks, and timeline – essentially creating a miniature Gantt chart in text form.
技巧 : 直接提示產生一個包含階段、任務和時間線的專案計畫大綱，基本上是在文字形式中建立一個簡化的甘特圖。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A project roadmap. For an e-commerce site example, you might get:
結果 : 一個專案路線圖。以電商網站為例，你可能會得到：
    

    

      Planning (Week 1-2):
       Gathering requirements, defining scope, and designing mockups.
規劃 (第 1-2 週)：收集需求、定義範圍，並設計原型。 
    

    

      Development (Week 3-8)
      : Set up the front-end framework, implement the product catalog, and integrate the payment gateway (6 weeks).
開發 (第 3-8 週) ：建立前端框架，實作產品目錄，並整合支付閘道 (6 週)。 
    

    

      Testing (Week 9-10)
      : QA testing of all features and bug fixes (2 weeks).
測試 (第 9-10 週) ：所有功能的 QA 測試與錯誤修復 (2 週)。 
    

    

      Pre-Launch (Week 11)
      : Content load, final reviews, soft launch for internal team.
預發佈 (第 11 週) ：載入內容、最終審核，並對內部團隊進行軟發佈。
    

    

      Launch (Week 12):
       Go live, monitor issues and marketing kickoff.
啟動 (第 12 週)：正式上線、監測問題及行銷啟動。
    

    

      This tangible timeline can be used to communicate with the team or stakeholders. It turns a goal into a series of actionable chunks with timeframes. Of course, one would refine it, but as a starting point, it’s beneficial.
這個具體的時間軸可以用來與團隊或利害相關者溝通。它將目標轉化為一系列有時間範疇的可執行任務。當然，之後還會進行細化，但作為起點，這是有幫助的。
    

    

      Crisis Management Plan
危機應變計畫 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our company just experienced [crisis scenario] (e.g., a data breach of customer information). Outline a crisis management plan for the next 48 hours. Include immediate steps to contain/resolve the issue, communication steps (internal and external), and any short-term measures to support affected stakeholders. Bullet points or a step list is fine.”
提示：「我們公司剛剛遭遇了 [危機情境]（例如：客戶資訊資料洩漏）。請列出未來 48 小時的危機應變計畫。包含立即的措施以控制/解決問題、溝通步驟（內部與外部），以及任何短期措施來支持受影響的利害相關者。使用項目符號或步驟清單皆可。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt focusing on urgent action plan with specific categories (containment, communication, support).
技巧：直接提示著重於緊急應變計畫，包含特定類別（封鎖、溝通、支援）。 
    

    

      Outcome
      : A clear list of urgent actions. For a data breach example:
成果：明確的緊急行動清單。以資料外洩為例：
    

    

      Containment
      : e.g., “Immediately secure servers, change access credentials, involve IT security team to stop the breach.”
封鎖：例如，「立即 securing 伺服器，變更存取憑證，動員資訊安全團隊以停止外洩。」
    

    

      Assessment
      : “Identity data compromised and the extent of the breach within the first 4 hours.”
評估：「在前 4 小時內確認身分資料遭竊取及外洩範圍。」
    

    

      Internal Communication
      : “Notify the executive team and relevant employees about the breach and actions underway.”
內部溝通 : 「通知執行團隊及相關員工關於資料外洩事件及目前進行的處理措施。」
    

    

      External Communication
      : “Within 24 hours, prepare a public statement and an email to affected customers acknowledging the issue and our response plan.”
外部溝通 : 「在 24 小時內，準備一份公開聲明及寄送電子郵件給受影響的客戶，說明問題並告知我們的應對計畫。」
    

    

      Legal
      : “Inform legal/regulatory bodies if required (e.g., GDPR authorities within 72 hours).”
法務 : 「如需告知法規監管機關（例如：72 小時內通知 GDPR 相關單位）。」
    

    

      Support
      : “Set up a customer support hotline/response team for queries or assistance to affected users.”
支援 : 「設立客戶支援專線/應變小組，以處理受影響用戶的查詢或協助需求。」
    

    

      Next 48 hours
      : “Begin an investigation (root cause analysis), plan longer-term security patches, schedule a press briefing if needed,” etc.
接下來 48 小時 :「開始調查（根本原因分析）、規劃長期的安全補丁、如需要則安排記者會」等。
    

    

      Such an output serves as a checklist in stressful times when clarity is needed. It ensures you cover key bases: fix, inform, and prevent future harm.
這樣的輸出在壓力大的時候能作為檢查清單，提供清晰的指引。它確保你覆蓋關鍵重點：修復、通報，並預防未來的損害。
    

    

      Product Roadmap Brainstorm
產品路線圖腦力激盪
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We have a software product in [brief domain]. Propose a 6-month product roadmap with 3-5 new features or improvements. For each feature, briefly describe and explain why it’s important (e.g., meets what user needs or strategic goals). Also, prioritize them (which to do first).”
提示 :「我們有一個在 [簡要領域] 的軟體產品。請提出一個 6 個月的產品路線圖，包含 3-5 個新功能或改進。每個功能請簡要描述並說明其重要性（例如，符合哪些用戶需求或戰略目標）。同時，請優先排序（哪些功能應先執行）。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt for roadmap planning, asking for features + justification + prioritization.
技術 : 直接提示進行路線圖規劃，要求功能 + 理由 + 優先順序。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A mini product roadmap. For example, for a project management app, features might be:
結果 : 一個簡化的產品路線圖。例如，對於專案管理應用程式，功能可能包括：
    

    

      Mobile App Version
       – 
      Description
      : Allow users to manage tasks on the go with iOS/Android apps. Importance: High user demand and improved accessibility are likely to increase engagement. 
行動應用程式版本 – 描述 : 允許使用者透過 iOS/Android 應用程式在移動端管理任務。重要性：高使用者需求與提升可近性將可能提高參與度。
    

    

      Priority:
       1 (first, as it expands user base).
優先順序：1（第一優先，因為這能擴展使用者群）。
    

    

      Team Dashboard
       – 
團隊看板 – 
    

    

      Description
      : An overview dashboard showing project status across teams. Importance: Helps managers get quick insights and sets us apart from competitors. 
      Priority:
       2.
說明 : 顯示各團隊專案狀態的總覽看板。重要性 : 帮助管理者快速掌握情況，並與競爭對手區隔。優先順序 : 2。
    

    

      Integration with Slack
       – 
與 Slack 整合 – 
    

    

      Description
      : Two-way integration to get notifications and add tasks via Slack. Importance: Enhances workflow for users and taps into common tool usage. 
說明 : 兩向整合以接收通知並透過 Slack 新增任務。重要性 : 提升用戶的工作流程，並善用常見的工具。
    

    

      Priority:
       3 (can be later as it’s an enhancement).
優先級：3（可以稍後進行，因為這是功能增強）。 
    

    

      This gives a clear plan of what to build, why, and in what order – extremely valuable for aligning the team and communicating with stakeholders. It’s a tangible outcome that guides the development focus.
這提供了一個明確的建設計畫，說明要建什麼、為何要建，以及順序 – 對於團隊協調與與利害關係人溝通極為寶貴。這是一項具體的成果，能引導開發重點。
    

    

      Cost-Cutting Suggestions
節省成本建議 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our expenses have been higher than expected in [area, e.g., marketing or operations]. Suggest five cost-cutting ideas to reduce expenses without significantly hurting quality or revenue. For each idea, include a quick note on how to implement it. Be practical and consider employee/customer impact.”
提示：「我們在[領域，例如行銷或運營]的開支高於預期。請提出五個節省成本的點子，以減少開支而不顯著影響品質或收入。每個點子請包含一個簡短的實施說明。請務必實用，並考慮對員工或客戶的影響。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt for cost-saving ideas, emphasizing practicality and minimal negative impact.
技巧 : 直接提問節省成本的點子，強調實用性與最小的負面影響。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A list of cost reduction initiatives. If the area is marketing, for example:
成果 : 一連串的成本降低方案。例如在行銷領域：
    

    

      “Optimize Ad Spend – Analyze digital ad campaigns and cut spend on low-performing keywords/ads. Implement by reviewing the ROI of each campaign monthly and reallocating the budget to top performers.”
「優化廣告支出 – 分析數位廣告活動，減少低績效關鍵字或廣告的支出。透過每月檢視各個活動的投資回報率（ROI），並將預算重新分配至表現最佳的項目。」
    

    

      “Use More Organic Marketing – Shift focus to content marketing/SEO and social media (free or low-cost) instead of expensive paid channels. Implement by investing in a content creator who can boost our blog and social presence.”
「使用更多自然行銷 – 將重點轉向內容行銷/SEO 與社交媒體（免費或低成本）而非昂貴的付費管道。透過投資內容創作者來提升我們的部落格與社交媒體能見度。」
    

    

      “Negotiation with Vendors – Renegotiate contracts with marketing software vendors or switch to cheaper alternatives. Implementation: contact each vendor for discounts or consider open-source tools where possible.”
「與供應商談判 – 重新協商與行銷軟體供應商的契約，或轉換至較便宜的替代方案。執行方式：與每個供應商洽談折扣，或在可能的情況下考慮使用開源工具。」
    

    

      “In-house Creative – Reduce outsourcing to agencies for creatives; do more design and copy in-house. Implement by training current staff or using inexpensive freelance platforms as needed.”
「內製創意 – 減少委外至代理商的創意工作；多在內部進行設計與文案。執行方式：透過培訓現有員工，或在需要時使用廉價的自由職業者平台。」
    

    

      “Referrals/Word-of-Mouth Program – Encourage customer referrals that cost less per acquisition (give small incentives instead of spending on ads). Implement by launching a referral bonus program.”
「推薦/口碑計畫 – 鼓勵顧客推薦，以降低獲客成本（提供小額獎勵，而非廣告支出）。執行方式：啟動推薦獎金計畫。」
    

    

      Each idea has an implementation tip, making it actionable. These can directly feed into a cost-saving plan or discussion with the team.
每個點子都附有執行建議，使其更具行動力。這些建議可直接納入節省成本計畫或與團隊討論中。
    

    

      Cross-Cultural Communication Tips
跨文化溝通技巧 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “Our team will work with a partner company from [country/culture]. Provide a brief guide with five tips on respecting cultural norms and communicating effectively with colleagues from this culture. Include do’s or don’ts in business etiquette, communication style, or any relevant custom we should be aware of.”
Prompt : 「我們的團隊將與來自[國家/文化]的合夥公司合作。請提供一個簡短的指南，包含五個關於尊重文化規範並有效與該文化背景的同事溝通的技巧。請包含在商業禮儀、溝通方式或任何我們應注意的相關習俗中的應做或應避免的行為。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt for cultural etiquette advice, listing actionable tips.
Technique : 直接請求文化禮儀建議，列出可執行的技巧。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A cultural etiquette guide snippet. For example, if working with a Japanese partner:
Outcome : 一個文化禮儀指南片段。例如，若與日本合夥公司合作：
    

    

      “
      Respect Formality
      : Use formal titles and surnames unless invited to use first names. Don’t be overly casual in emails or meetings initially​.”
尊重禮儀：除非被邀請使用名字，否則應使用正式的頭銜與姓氏。在電子郵件或會議初期，不要過於隨便。  
    

    

      “
      Communication Style
      : Be attentive to non-verbal cues and pauses – silence can be a sign of careful consideration, not disagreement. Avoid interrupting, as it’s seen as rude.”
溝通方式：留意非語言的暗示與停頓 – 沉默可能是仔細思考的跡象，而非不同意。避免打斷他人，這會被視為不禮貌。  
    

    

      “
      Decision-Making
      : Expect that decisions might be made by consensus. It’s good to be patient through deliberations and not push for immediate answers in meetings.”
決策方式：預期決策可能由共識產生。在會議中，應耐心參與討論，不要急著要求立即的答案。  
    

    

      “
      Business Cards (Meishi
      ): Exchange business cards with both hands and take a moment to read the card you receive. Treat it respectfully (don’t write on it or shove it in your pocket).”
名片（Meishi）：交換名片時應使用雙手，並花點時間閱讀對方給你的名片。應當尊重名片（不要在上面寫字或隨便塞進口袋）。
    

    

      “Punctuality
      : Being on time is very important. Arrive a few minutes early for meetings as a sign of respect.”
準時：守時非常重要。與會時提前幾分鐘到達，是表示尊重的象徵。
    

    

      Each tip is concrete. This tangible output can be shared with your team before the engagement, helping avoid faux pas and building smoother relationships.
每個提示都非常具體。這種可見的成果可以於參與前與團隊分享，有助於避免失禮情況，並建立更順暢的關係。
    

    

      Customer Satisfaction KPIs
客戶滿意度 KPIs
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We want to measure and improve customer satisfaction. Propose three key performance indicators (KPIs) that we should track for customer satisfaction, explaining briefly how each KPI reflects satisfaction. For each KPI, suggest how we might collect the data (e.g., surveys, support tickets) and an example target or benchmark.”
Prompt : 「我們想要衡量並提升客戶滿意度。請提出三個我們應該追蹤的客戶滿意度關鍵績效指標（KPIs），並簡要說明每個 KPI 如何反映滿意度。針對每個 KPI，請建議我們如何收集數據（例如：問卷、客服 ticket），並提供一個目標或基准值的範例。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Direct prompt for metric identification, with explanation and implementation.
技巧：直接提示以識別指標，並附說明與實作方式。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A set of customer satisfaction metrics with context. For example:
成果：具備情境的客戶滿意度指標。例如：
    

    

      Net Promoter Score (NPS):
Net Promoter Score (NPS)：
       
    

    

      Explanation
      : This measure indicates the likelihood of customers recommending us and indicates overall satisfaction/loyalty. It is collected via post-purchase or periodic surveys asking “How likely to recommend… (0-10).” Target: For example, aim for an NPS of +50, which is above the industry average.
說明：此指標顯示客戶推薦我們的可能性，並反映整體滿意度與忠誠度。透過購後或定期問卷收集，問題為「您有多大可能性會推薦我們？（0-10）」。目標：例如，目標為達到 +50 的 NPS，這高於產業平均值。
    

    

      Customer Satisfaction (CSAT) Score: 
客戶滿意度（CSAT）分數：
    

    

      Explanation
      : Direct rating of a specific interaction or purchase (e.g., “Rate your experience 1-5”). Reflects immediate satisfaction. Collection: short feedback surveys right after customer support chats or product delivery. Target: 90% of responses 4 or 5 out of 5.
說明：針對特定互動或購買進行直接評分（例如：「請對您的經驗進行 1 到 5 分評分」）。反映即時的滿意程度。收集方式：在客服對話或產品交付後立即進行短問卷調查。目標：90%的回應評分為 4 或 5 分。
    

    

      First Contact Resolution Rate: Explanation
      : The percentage of support issues resolved on the first attempt—higher means customers get their issues solved quickly, a satisfaction driver. Collection: Track support ticket data. Target: e.g., 85% one-touch resolution reduces repeat contacts and frustration.
首次接觸解決率：說明：首次嘗試即解決支持問題的百分比——越高表示客戶的問題能快速得到解決，是滿意度的驅動因素。收集方式：追蹤支持工單資料。目標：例如，85%的一鍵解決率可減少重複聯繫與不滿情緒。
    

    

      These are tangible metrics for starting a customer satisfaction program, complete with instructions on how to measure and what good looks like.
這些是啟動客戶滿意度計畫的具體指標，並附有如何衡量以及什麼是良好表現的說明。
    

    

      Benchmarking Plan
基准計畫 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “We want to benchmark our performance against industry standards. Outline a brief plan on how to do this: what key metrics we should compare, where to find industry benchmark data for those metrics, and how to present the comparison to our team. Provide 3-4 steps or recommendations.”
提示 : 「我們想要將我們的表現與產業標準做比較。請簡要說明如何進行這個比較：我們應該比較哪些關鍵指標、在哪裡可以找到這些指標的產業基准數據，以及如何向我們的團隊呈現比較結果。請提供 3-4 個步驟或建議。」
    

    

      Technique
      : A planning prompt that asks for metrics selection, data sources, and communication – all elements of a benchmarking initiative.
技巧 : 一個計畫提示，要求說明指標選擇、數據來源以及溝通方式 —— 所有屬於基准計畫的要素。
    

    

      Outcome
      : An actionable benchmarking plan. For example:
結果 : 一個可執行的基准計畫。例如：
    

    

      “
      Identify Metrics
      : Focus on metrics like customer acquisition cost (CAC), conversion rate, churn rate, and profit margin that are crucial to our business and commonly benchmarked in our industry.
識別關鍵指標：專注於對我們業務至關重要的指標，如客戶獲取成本（CAC）、轉化率、客戶流失率及利潤率，這些指標在我們的產業中常被用作比較基准。
    

    

      Gather Industry Data
      : Use industry reports from sources like Gartner or IBISWorld for broad metrics; look at published studies or competitor public data (annual reports for margins, etc.); subscribe to industry associations or use tools like Google’s Market Insights for specific stats. Additionally, services like Benchmarks by Google Analytics (for web metrics) or SaaS benchmarking reports (if we’re SaaS) can provide data​.
蒐集產業數據：使用來自 Gartner 或 IBISWorld 等來源的產業報告來取得廣泛的指標數據；查看已發表的研究報告或競爭對手公開的數據（如年度報告中的利潤率等）；訂閱產業協會或使用 Google 的 Market Insights 等工具來取得特定的統計數據。此外，像 Google Analytics 的 Benchmarks 服務（用於網頁指標）或 SaaS 行業的比較報告（如果我們是 SaaS 公司）也能提供數據。
    

    

      Compare and Analyze
      : Create a table comparing our metrics to industry averages or top quartile numbers. Highlight areas where we exceed benchmarks (to celebrate) and where we lag (opportunities for improvement). Ensure data is time-aligned (e.g., use last year’s data for us and the industry if the current year is not out yet).
比較與分析：製作一個比較我們的指標與產業平均值或前 25% 指標的表格。標註我們超越基准的部分（值得慶祝）以及落後的部分（改進機會）。確保數據時間對應（例如，如果當前年度數據尚未公布，則使用去年的數據進行比較）。
    

    

      Present to Team
      : Visualize the comparison (bar charts for each metric). Emphasize that this is to identify improvement areas, not to assign blame. Discuss possible reasons for differences – e.g., if our CAC is higher, maybe our marketing spend strategy differs – and brainstorm actions to close gaps or leverage strengths.”
對團隊說明：將比較結果視覺化（每個指標使用條形圖）。強調這項比較是為了找出改進的空間，而非歸咎責任。討論差異可能的原因 – 例如，如果我們的 CAC 較高，可能是行銷花費策略不同 – 並集思廣益找出縮小差距或善用優勢的行動。
    

    

      This output clearly outlines what to do and how to do it. It’s tangible advice on executing a benchmarking project.
這個輸出清楚說明了該做什麼以及如何做。這是具體的建議，說明如何執行一個基准分析專案。
    

    

      Conflict Resolution Role-Play
衝突解決角色扮演 
    

    

      Prompt
      : “There’s a conflict between two team members over [issue]. Role-play a coaching conversation where I (as their manager) talk to one of them (Employee A) to help resolve the conflict. Include me asking about their perspective, acknowledging their feelings, guiding them to see the other’s viewpoint, and collaboratively finding a solution. Provide the dialogue in a script form (Manager and Employee A lines).”
提示：「兩位團隊成員之間有關於[問題]的衝突。請進行一場角色扮演，模擬我（作為他們的主管）與其中一位員工（員工 A）的對話，協助解決衝突。請包含我詢問員工 A 的觀點、承認他們的感受、引導他們理解對方的立場，並共同尋找解決方案。請以對話腳本形式呈現（主管與員工 A 的對話內容）。」
    

    

      Technique
      : Role-play prompts the AI to produce a sample dialogue for a sensitive management situation.
技巧：角色扮演促使 AI 產生一個敏感管理情境的對話範例。
    

    

      Outcome
      : A scripted conversation that demonstrates effective conflict-resolution techniques. For example:
結果：一個腳本對話，展現有效的衝突解決技巧。例如：
    

    

      Manager:
       “Thanks for sitting with me, [Employee A]. I wanted to discuss the issues between you and [Employee B]. Can you share how you see the situation?”
經理：「謝謝你願意坐下來和我談，[員工 A]。我想和你討論你和[員工 B]之間的問題。你能說說你對這件事情的看法嗎？」
    

    

      Employee A:
       “Honestly, I feel like I’m being blamed for the project delay, but I was waiting on data from B…”
員工 A：「坦白說，我覺得自己被怪罪了專案延誤，但其實我在等 B 提供的資料……」
    

    

      Manager:
       “I understand. It sounds like you’re frustrated because you were depending on late information. Is that right?”
經理：「我了解。聽起來你是因為依賴晚到的資訊而感到不滿，對嗎？」 
    

    

      Employee A:
       “Exactly, I felt stuck.”
員工 A：「確實，我覺得進退兩難。」 
    

    

      Manager:
       “That’s understandable. And I’ve heard B’s perspective, too – they felt pressured by the tight timeline. It seems both of you were under stress. What can we do to improve communication if this happens again?”
經理：「可以理解。我也聽過 B 的觀點 – 他們覺得時間太緊迫而感到壓力。看來你們兩人都有壓力。如果再發生這種情況，我們可以做些什麼來改善溝通呢？」 
    

    

      Employee A:
       “Maybe B and I need to agree on interim check-ins…”
員工 A：「或許 B 和我需要約定一些中間的檢查點……」
    

    

      Manager:
      
         “That’s a great idea... etc.”
        
經理：「那是個好主意... 等等。」

        The conversation would go on to find a resolution or mutual understanding. This is a tangible tool – a manager could practice with it or take lines from it. It models a calm, empathetic approach to conflict resolution.
      
對話將持續進行，以找到解決方案或達成共識。這是一個實體工具，經理可以拿來練習或引用其中的對話內容。它模擬了一種冷靜、富有同理心的衝突解決方式。
    

    

      Advanced AI Prompts for Personal & Business Effectiveness
個人與商業效能的高階 AI 提示
    

    

      Personal Systems & Productivity
個人系統與生產力
    

    

      Use AI to build custom systems that organize your life and work. These prompts create structured plans and routines tailored to your goals and habits.
使用 AI 來建立客製化系統，以整理你的生活與工作。這些提示可以創造出結構化的計畫與例行程序，根據你的目標與習慣進行調整。
    

    

      “TracyOS” Time Management System: 
「TracyOS」時間管理系統：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “You are my AI productivity assistant, TracyOS, designed to help manage my time based on my values and goals. First, ask me about my top priorities, recurring tasks, and long-term objectives. Then create a personalized daily schedule optimizing my time allocation (using principles from time-management expert Brian Tracy). Include prioritized tasks, realistic time blocks, breaks, and strategies to handle distractions (I have ADHD tendencies). Finally, present the plan with a brief explanation of how it aligns to my goals.”
完整提示：「你是我的 AI 生產力助手 TracyOS，設計用來根據我的價值觀和目標來管理我的時間。首先，請問我的首要優先事項、重複性任務以及長期目標。然後建立一個個人化的每日行程，優化我的時間配置（運用時間管理專家 Brian Tracy 的原則）。包含優先任務、現實可行的時間區塊、休息時間以及處理分心的策略（我有 ADHD 傾向）。最後，以簡短的說明呈現這個計畫，並說明它如何與我的目標對應。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Setting up a comprehensive daily planning system that keeps someone focused on high-value tasks. 
使用案例：建立一個全面的每日計畫系統，讓某人專注於高價值任務。
    

    

      Optimized for:
       GPT-4 (best for nuanced scheduling advice) on ChatGPT. 
      Context:
       This prompt (inspired by a community-designed “TracyOS” tool ) acts as an operating system for your day, helping create a time management plan tailored to you.
優化用於：GPT-4（最適合提供細膩的排程建議）在 ChatGPT 上。情境：這個提示（靈感來自社區設計的「TracyOS」工具）就像是你一天的作業系統，幫助你建立一個符合個人需求的時間管理計畫。
    

    

      Daily Schedule & Goal Tracker: 
每日排程與目標追蹤：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Based on my 2025 goals and vision for an ideal life, create a daily schedule that reflects my dream day. Include time blocks for work, study, leisure, health, and family, aligning each block to a specific goal or value. Build in buffer time for unexpected delays and some ‘dopamine breaks’ for motivation. Present the schedule as a timetable, and briefly explain how each part supports my goals.”
完整提示：「根據我的 2025 目標與對理想生活的願景，建立一個反映我夢想一天的每日排程。包含工作、學習、休閒、健康與家庭的時間區塊，並將每個區塊與特定目標或價值觀對應。預留緩衝時間以應對突發的延誤，並加入一些「多巴胺短暫休息」來提升動機。以時間表的方式呈現這個排程，並簡要說明每個部分如何支持我的目標。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Designing an ideal day structure that balances long-term goals with daily needs. 
使用情境：設計一個理想一天的結構，平衡長期目標與日常需求。
    

    

      Optimized for:
       ChatGPT (GPT-4 or 3.5). 
      Example:
       This prompt helps translate big goals into a realistic daily routine – e.g. if a goal is writing a book, the schedule will reserve a morning block for focused writing, with explanations why that time optimizes creativity.
優化用於：ChatGPT（GPT-4 或 3.5）。範例：這個提示能幫助將大目標轉化為現實的日常計畫 – 例如，如果目標是寫一本書，這個計畫會為專注寫作預留一個早晨的時間段，並說明為何那個時間點能最佳化創造力。
    

    

      90-Day Personal Development Planner: 
90 天個人發展計畫：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Assume you are a personal development coach. Given my strengths (e.g., communication, creativity) and weaknesses (e.g., procrastination, inconsistency), create a 90-day improvement plan. Outline specific weekly goals and actionable steps for each area I want to improve. Include milestones at 30, 60, and 90 days, and strategies to overcome obstacles (like loss of motivation or distractions) that might occur.”
完整提示：「假設你是個人發展教練。根據我的優勢（例如：溝通能力、創造力）和弱點（例如：拖延、不一致），制定一個 90 天的改進計畫。列出每個想要改進領域的具體週目標和可執行的步驟。包含 30 天、60 天和 90 天的里程碑，並說明如何克服可能出現的障礙（例如：動力消失或分心）」。
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Turning self-improvement goals (like building a habit or learning a skill) into a structured action plan. 
使用情境：將自我提升目標（例如建立習慣或學習技能）轉化為結構化的行動計畫。
    

    

      Optimized for
       GPT-4 (for detailed, insightful plans) on ChatGPT or Claude. 
      Context:
       This prompt yields a step-by-step personal growth roadmap, essentially acting as a life coach in structuring your next three months (inspired by community-shared prompts for goal setting ).
為 GPT-4 優化（用於詳細且有洞察力的計畫）於 ChatGPT 或 Claude。情境：此提示可產生逐步的個人成長路線圖，基本上就如同一位人生顧問，協助你規劃接下來的三個月（靈感來自社群共享的目標設定提示）。
    

    

      Decision Clarity & Strategic Thinking
決策清晰度與策略思考
    

    

      When facing big decisions or complex problems, these prompts leverage AI to provide clarity, critical analysis, and diverse perspectives for better choices.
面對重大決策或複雜問題時，這些提示利用 AI 提供清晰度、批判性分析與多樣化的觀點，以做出更好的選擇。
    

    

      Virtual Board of Advisors Simulation: 
虛擬顧問委員會模擬：
    

    

      Full Prompt:
       
      “You are a panel of five experts I admire (a ‘virtual board of advisors’). The members are: [List 3–5 names or roles, e.g., ‘Steve Jobs (innovation), Indra Nooyi (strategy), an ADHD productivity coach, a Harvard professor, and my future self’]. They are gathered to advise me on 
      [describe your decision or challenge]
      . Simulate a discussion where each advisor offers perspective, asks insightful questions, and debates the best solution. Finally, have the panel reach a consensus recommendation and summarize the reasoning from each perspective.”
「您是五位我欽佩的專家組成的委員會（一個「虛擬顧問團」）。成員包括：[列出 3-5 個名字或角色，例如：「Steve Jobs（創新）、Indra Nooyi（策略）、ADHD 生產力教練、哈佛大學教授，以及我的未來自己」]。他們聚會來為我提供關於[描述您的決定或挑戰]的建議。模擬一場討論，每位顧問提供他們的觀點，提出深入的問題，並辯論最佳解決方案。最後，讓這個委員會達成共識性的建議，並總結每個觀點的理由。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Getting well-rounded advice on a tough decision (career move, product strategy, life choice) by hearing it critiqued from multiple angles. 
使用情境：透過聆聽來自多個角度的批評，獲得全面的建議，來處理一個困難的決定（如職業轉變、產品策略、人生選擇）。
    

    

      Optimized for
       GPT-4 (for maintaining distinct personas in one response) or Claude (for lengthy, detailed discussions). 
      Context:
       This prompt creates a “dream team” meeting in text, allowing you to 
      “pick the brains”
       of mentors or even fictional archetypes. It helps surface diverse ideas you might not consider alone, enhancing decision-making with breadth and depth.
針對 GPT-4 優化（用以維持一個回應中不同的個性），或針對 Claude 優化（用以進行長篇且詳細的討論）。情境：這個提示創造了一個「夢幻團隊」的會議形式，讓您可以「請教」導師或甚至是虛構的象徵人物。它有助於挖掘出您獨自可能不會考慮的多樣想法，以廣度與深度來提升決策品質。
    

    

      “Brutal VC” Devil’s Advocate Critique: 
「Brutal VC」魔鬼代言人批評：
    

    

      Full Prompt:
       
      “Act as a ruthless venture capitalist evaluating a proposal. I will describe my business idea and want you to tear it apart with surgical precision. 
完整提示：「請扮演一位殘忍的風險投資人，評估一個提案。我會說明我的商業點子，請你以手術刀般的精準度來剖析它。
    

    

      Critically analyze every flaw, assumption, and risk in the idea as if you’re trying to 
      convince me not to invest
      . Be brutally honest and detail the weaknesses in the market, product, business model, execution, etc. 
以批判的角度分析這個點子的每個缺陷、假設與風險，就像你試圖說服我不要投資一樣。請誠實且詳細地指出市場、產品、商業模式、執行等各方面的弱點。
    

    

      Then suggest what must change to make the idea more viable.”
然後提出必須做出哪些改變，才能讓這個點子更具可行性。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Pressure-testing a startup idea or project plan by identifying pitfalls and areas of improvement. 
使用情境：透過識別潛在的問題與改進空間，來壓力測試一個創業點子或專案計畫。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (GPT-4) or Claude (both can deliver a thorough critique; GPT-4 tends to be more nuanced in harsh feedback). 
為 ChatGPT（GPT-4）或 Claude 優化使用（兩者都能提供深入的評論；GPT-4 在給予嚴厲反饋時較為細膩）。 
    

    

      Example:
       Entrepreneurs can input their business concept and receive an unfiltered critique that friends or colleagues might shy away from. This prompt forces you to confront hard truths and refine your idea—essentially a 
      risk assessment
       through an adversarial lens.
範例：創業者可以輸入自己的商業點子，並獲得朋友或同事可能不敢給予的直接評論。這個提示迫使你面對嚴峻的事實，並精進你的想法—簡而言之，就是透過對立的視角進行風險評估。 
    

    

      Project Pre-Mortem Analyzer: 
專案預先遺憾分析工具： 
    

    

      Full Prompt:
       
      “Imagine we are one year in the future, and 
      [my project or decision]
       has 
      failed spectacularly
      . As a post-mortem analysis expert, list the top reasons (internal or external) that could have led to this failure. For each potential reason, I propose a preventive measure or contingency plan I could implement to mitigate that risk. Present the results as a ‘failure scenario’ list with its corresponding solution.”
完整提示：「假設我們在一 year 後，[我的專案或決定] 已經慘敗。作為遺憾分析專家，列出導致這個失敗的前五大原因（內部或外部）。對於每個可能的原因，我提出相應的預防措施或應變計畫，以降低該風險。將結果以「遺憾情境」清單搭配對應的解決方案呈現。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Identifying risks and weaknesses 
      before
       starting a project or making an important decision allows you to address them in advance. 
使用情境：在開始一個專案或做出重要決定前識別風險與弱點，可以讓你提前處理這些問題。
    

    

      Optimized for ChatGPT (GPT-4) or Claude, it
       
      works especially well in DeepSeek
       if you want to pull in real-world examples of similar failures. 
優化用於 ChatGPT (GPT-4) 或 Claude，如果你想要引入類似失敗的現實案例，尤其適合在 DeepSeek 上使用。
    

    

      Context:
       This prompt turns the AI into a risk management consultant using the pre-mortem technique popularized in business. It yields a frank list of “what could go wrong” and actionable fixes, improving strategic foresight.
脈絡：這個提示將 AI 轉化為風險管理顧問，運用在商業界廣為流行的預-mortem 技術。它能產生一張坦率的「什麼可能會出錯」清單，並提供可執行的解決方案，提升戰略預見能力。
    

    

      ADHD-Friendly Planning & Work Aids
ADHD 友善型規劃與工作輔助工具
    

    

      For those with ADHD or neurodivergent work styles, these prompts are tailored to boost focus, breakthrough executive dysfunction, and maintain motivation in unique ways.
對於有 ADHD 或神經多樣工作風格的人，這些提示是根據個人需求設計，以提升專注力、突破執行功能障礙，並以獨特的方式維持動機。
    

    

      Task Breakdown Wizard:
       
      Full Prompt:
       
      “Break down this overwhelming task: 
      [describe the project or big task]
      , into a sequence of ultra-manageable steps (5-10 minute micro-tasks). The steps should be so small and specific that they bypass any executive function overload. Begin each step with an action verb and ensure each feels easy to start.”
任務分解魔術師：完整提示：「將這個令人感到壓力的任務：[描述專案或大任務]，分解成一系列極易管理的步驟（5-10 分鐘的微任務）。這些步驟應當非常小且具體，以避免任何執行功能過載。每個步驟都應以動作動詞開頭，並確保每個步驟都感覺容易開始。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Overcoming procrastination on big or intimidating tasks by slicing them into tiny, non-intimidating actions. 
使用情境：透過將大任務或令人畏懼的任務切割成微小、不具威脅性的行動，來克服拖延。
    

    

      Optimized for:
       ChatGPT (any model) or Claude. 
      Context:
       This prompt helps ADHD brains create momentum by starting with very small wins. For example, 
      “Step 1: Open the project folder. Step 2: Create a new document named… etc.”
       – trivial steps that build progress . It’s derived from ADHD communities emphasizing that 
      micro-steps
       can “bypass executive function challenges”.
最佳適用：ChatGPT（任何模型）或 Claude。情境：此提示協助 ADHD 大腦建立動力，從非常小的成就開始。例如：「步驟 1：打開專案資料夾。步驟 2：建立一個名為……的新文件等。」——這些微不足道的步驟能逐步建立進展。此提示源自於 ADHD 社群強調「微小步驟可以繞過執行功能的挑戰」。
    

    

      Dopamine-Friendly Scheduler: 
多巴胺友善排程： 
    

    

      Full Prompt:
       
      “I have a list of tasks to do: [paste your tasks]. As an ADHD-friendly planner, I reorganize my task list into a schedule that will keep me engaged. Alternate between high-effort tasks and more fun or easy tasks to create natural dopamine breaks. Also, incorporate a short reward (like a snack, song, or quick game) after I complete a difficult task. Present a timeline for the day that balances productivity and stimulation.”
完整提示：「我有一個待辦事項清單：[貼上你的待辦事項]。作為一個 ADHD 友善的規劃者，我會重新整理我的待辦事項清單，製成一個能讓我保持專注的排程。在高強度任務與較有趣或較容易的任務之間交替，以創造自然的多巴胺間歇。另外，在我完成困難任務後，加入一個短暫的獎勵（例如吃點心、聽一首歌或玩個快速遊戲）。呈現一個當天的時間軸，平衡生產力與刺激。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Making a daily plan that sustains motivation by weaving in variety and rewards – preventing burnout or boredom. 
使用情境：製作一個當日計畫，透過加入多樣性與獎勵來維持動機 – 避免過度疲勞或感到無聊。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT or Claude (either can inject creative rewards and ordering). 
      Example:
       If an ADHD student must write an essay, study math, and do laundry, the AI might schedule: 
      “9:00–9:30: Write introduction paragraph (then 5-minute YouTube break); 9:35–10:00: Fold laundry (easy task); 10:00–10:45: Finish essay body (then treat yourself with a snack)”
      , etc. This keeps the brain’s reward system engaged.
最佳化用於 ChatGPT 或 Claude（任一都可以注入創意獎勵與順序）。例如：如果一個 ADHD 學生必須寫論文、學習數學和洗衣服，AI 可能會排程：「9:00–9:30：寫引言段落（然後 5 分鐘 YouTube 休息）；9:35–10:00：摺衣服（輕鬆任務）；10:00–10:45：完成論文正文（然後以點心作為獎勵）」，等等。這有助於維持大腦的獎勵系統活躍。
    

    

      Focus Environment Designer: 
專注環境設計師: 
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Act as an ADHD workplace consultant. I need to do deep work on [specific task]. Suggest an ideal work environment setup and protocol to maximize my focus. Consider lighting, sound or music, desk layout, and removing distractions. Include any tools or browser extensions that might help. Then outline a ‘focus session’ routine (e.g., 25-minute focus, 5-minute break cycles) tailored to an easily-distracted brain.”
完整提示：「請扮演一位 ADHD 職場顧問。我需要在[特定任務]上進行深度工作，請建議一個能最大化我專注力的理想工作環境設定與協議。請考慮照明、聲音或音樂、書桌擺放方式，以及去除干擾。包含任何可能有幫助的工具或瀏覽器擴充功能。然後說明一個為容易分心的腦所設計的「專注會話」流程（例如：25 分鐘專注、5 分鐘休息的循環）。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
