       Optimizing your physical or digital environment for concentration (useful for anyone, especially neurodivergent folks sensitive to surroundings). 
使用情境：優化你的物理或數位環境以提升專注力（對任何人皆有幫助，尤其是對環境敏感的神經多元人士）。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (GPT-4 for more varied suggestions). 
針對 ChatGPT 優化（使用 GPT-4 可獲得更多樣化的建議）。
    

    

      Context
      :
       This prompt produces practical tips like 
      “put phone in another room, use noise-canceling headphones with instrumental music, clear everything off your desk except one notepad,”
       etc., combined with a routine like the Pomodoro technique. It essentially creates an ADHD-friendly work protocol you can follow for a given task.
情境 : 這個提示會產生實用的建議，例如「把手機放在另一個房間，使用有背景音樂的降噪耳機，除了一個筆記本外清空桌面」等，並結合番茄工作法這樣的例行程序。它基本上會建立一個適合 ADHD 人士的工作協議，你可以用來執行特定任務。
    

    

      Time Blindness Navigator: 
時間盲導航者:
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “I struggle with time blindness when working on [activity] – I lose track of time and deadlines. As my time management coach, I develop strategies to manage this. Suggest perception-based timing techniques (like visual timers or alarms that give me a sense of passing time) rather than just relying on clocks. Also, I propose a way to externalize my schedule (calendars, apps, etc.) so I regularly see the timeframes. Provide a plan to keep me aware of time while I work.”
完整提示 : 「我在進行[活動]時會有時間盲的問題 – 我會忘記時間和截止日期。作為我的時間管理教練，我需要發展策略來管理這個問題。請建議基於感知的時間技巧（例如視覺計時器或警報器，讓我有時間流逝的感覺），而不是只依賴鐘錶。同時，我也希望有一種方法可以將我的日程外部化（日曆、應用程式等），讓我定期看到時間範圍。請提供一個計畫，讓我工作時能保持對時間的覺察。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Helping those who frequently “get in the zone” and miss time cues (familiar with ADHD) to stay aware of time passing. 
使用案例：協助那些經常「進入心流」而忽略時間訊號（熟悉 ADHD）的人，讓他們在工作時保持對時間流逝的覺察。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT or Claude. 
為 ChatGPT 或 Claude 優化。
    

    

      Context:
       This prompt yields a personalized anti-time-blindness plan, such as recommendations to use a Pomodoro timer with distinct sounds, calendar reminders that pop up, or even “narrate the time” habits. It directly addresses an ADHD pain point by introducing external structures to compensate for internal timing challenges.
情境：此提示可產生一個個人化的抗時間盲性計畫，例如建議使用有區別音效的番茄鐘、會彈出的行事曆提醒，甚至是「敘述時間」的習慣。它直接針對 ADHD 的痛點，透過引入外部結構來彌補內部時間管理的困難。
    

    

      Virtual Body Double for Focus: 
虛擬專注替身：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “I need a virtual body double to help me stay on task. Let’s work together on [task]. I will periodically tell you what I’m doing, and I want you to respond with brief encouragement, acknowledgment, or a gentle prompt to get back on task if I stray. Do not provide any unrelated information or long responses – just act like a supportive coworker quietly keeping me accountable in real-time.”
完整提示：「我需要一個虛擬專注替身來幫助我保持專注。我們一起來做[任務]。我會定期告訴你我在做什麼，而你則要以簡短的鼓勵、認可或輕柔的提醒來協助我回到任務上。不要提供任何不相關的資訊或長篇回應 – 只要像一個默默在實時中協助我保持責任感的支援同事。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Creating a sense of accountability and company while doing solo work – the AI acts as a silent partner, which is a known ADHD strategy called “body doubling” . 
使用情境：在獨自工作時建立責任感與專注度 – AI 會扮演一個沉默的夥伴角色，這是一種被廣為使用的 ADHD 策略，稱為「身體雙人法」（body doubling）。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (running continuously in a tab) or Claude; also well-suited to voice mode. 
      Example:
       A user might start: “Okay, I’m going to start drafting my report now.” The AI could reply, 
      “Great, I’m here with you… got your outline ready? 
      👍
      ”
      . Five minutes later, if the user hasn’t updated, it might gently ask, 
      “How is the introduction coming along?”
      . This keeps the person engaged and less likely to wander off mid-task.
最佳化於 ChatGPT（在分頁中持續運行）或 Claude；也適合語音模式。例如：使用者可能會開始說：「我現在要開始撰寫我的報告了。」AI 可以回應：「很好，我跟你一起在這裡… 你的大綱準備好了嗎？👍」五分鐘後，如果使用者沒有更新進度，AI 可能會溫和地詢問：「導言部分進行得如何？」這有助於維持使用者的專注，減少在任務中分心的可能。
    

    

      Executive Strategy & Entrepreneurship
執行策略與企業經營
    

    

      For entrepreneurs and professionals driving business growth, these prompts assist with high-level strategy, market analysis, and planning – going beyond generic advice into tailored actionable insights.
對於推動業務成長的企業家與專業人士，這些提示可協助進行高階策略、市場分析與規劃 – 超越一般性建議，提供針對性的可執行見解。
    

    

      Market Gap Analyzer (Business Strategist): 
市場缺口分析師（商業策略師）:
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Act as a business strategist and conduct a mini market analysis for [your industry or niche]. Identify any untapped opportunities or gaps in the market, given the current trends. Provide 2-3 specific ideas for new products or services that could fulfill the unmet needs of my target customers. For each idea, briefly explain why the market is underserved and what the unique value proposition could be.”
完整提示：「請扮演商業策略師，為[您的產業或利基市場]進行小型市場分析。根據當前趨勢，識別任何未被開發的機會或市場缺口。提供 2 至 3 個具體的新產品或服務點子，以滿足目標客戶的未被滿足需求。針對每個點子，簡要說明為何市場尚未被充分服務，以及其獨特價值主張為何。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Brainstorming new business ideas or expansion opportunities with data-driven insight. 
使用情境：腦力激盪新的商業點子或擴張機會，並結合數據驅動的洞察。
    

    

      Optimized for:
       
      DeepSeek
       (for live market data via web search) or GPT-4 with browsing enabled. 
      Context:
       This prompt yields innovative ideas grounded in real market gaps. It’s like having a consultant do quick market research – especially powerful if run on a platform that can fetch up-to-date industry info. For example, it might reveal a customer segment that competitors overlook and suggest a product to serve them.
最佳化於：DeepSeek（透過網頁搜尋取得即時市場資料）或啟用瀏覽功能的 GPT-4。情境：此提示能產生基於真實市場缺口的創新點子，就如同擁有顧問進行快速市場研究一般。特別是在能取得最新產業資訊的平台上執行，可能會發現競爭對手忽略的客戶群，並建議相應的產品來服務他們。
    

    

      Irresistible Offer Generator: 
無法抗拒的優惠生成器：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “I sell [your product or service]. Help me craft an irresistible offer around it. Outline the core product benefits, then add 2-3 valuable bonuses or complementary services that enhance the offer’s appeal. Clearly define the outcome or transformation the customer gets. Finally, suggest a concise tagline or value proposition to make my target customer say, ‘I need this now!’.”
完整提示：「我銷售 [您的產品或服務]。幫我打造一個無法抗拒的優惠。先列出核心產品的優點，然後加入 2-3 個有價值的附贈品或補充服務，以提升優惠的吸引力。明確說明客戶能獲得的結果或轉變。最後，建議一個簡潔有力的標語或價值主張，讓目標客戶說：「我現在就需要！」」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Improving a product/service bundle to boost sales and customer appeal (a common task for entrepreneurs launching or refining an offer). 
使用情境：改善產品或服務組合以提升銷售與客戶吸引力（這是創業者在推出或優化優惠時常見的任務）。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (GPT-4) or Claude. 
      Example:
       For an online course, the AI might suggest adding a free 1:1 coaching call and an e-book as bonuses, highlighting that “you’ll go from novice to skilled in 4 weeks,” and proposing a tagline like “Master [Skill] in One Month—Guaranteed.” This goes beyond basic copywriting by structuring the 
      offer
       itself to be more compelling (a technique shared in entrepreneur communities).
針對 ChatGPT (GPT-4) 或 Claude 進行優化。例如：對於線上課程，AI 可能建議加入免費的一對一輔導課程與電子書作為附贈，並強調「您將在四週內從新手進階為專業人士」，並提出標語如「一個月內精通 [技能] — 保證有效。」這種方法不僅超越基本的文案寫作，更透過結構化的方式讓優惠本身更具說服力（這是一種在創業者社群中廣為分享的技巧）。
    

    

      Content Strategy Architect:
       
內容策略架構師: 
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “You are a content marketing strategist. I want to grow my personal or business brand in [industry]. Design a 3-month content plan that increases my visibility and authority. Include a blogging strategy (topics for at least six blog posts), a social media plan (posting frequency and example post ideas for platforms like LinkedIn/Twitter), and one idea for a long-form piece (e.g., a whitepaper, webinar, or video). Make sure the content themes resonate with [my target audience or niche] and build toward a consistent message. Provide the plan in a timeline format.”
完整提示 : 「你是一位內容行銷策略師。我想要在[產業]領域建立個人或企業品牌，請設計一個 3 個月的內容計畫，以提升我的能見度與權威性。包含一個部落格策略（至少六篇部落格文章的主題），一個社交媒體計畫（如 LinkedIn/Twitter 等平台的發文頻率與範例發文點子），以及一個長篇內容的點子（例如白皮書、網路研討會或影片）。請確保內容主題能與[我的目標受眾或利基市場]產生共鳴，並朝向一致的訊息發展。請以時間軸格式提供計畫。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Quickly generating a structured content marketing plan, which entrepreneurs and small business owners often need for thought leadership or promotion. 
使用情境: 快速產生一個結構化的內容行銷計畫，這通常是創業者與小型企業主在建立思維領導或推廣品牌時所需要的。
    

    

      Optimized for
       Claude (for more extended output) or GPT-4. 
      Context:
       This prompt functions like a marketing consultant’s output. For example, it might output: 
      “Month 1: Publish blog on X, Y; Tweet daily tips; Month 2: LinkedIn articles on Z; short video about Q…**”
       etc., ensuring all content reinforces your brand narrative. It’s a high-level strategy that can then be executed piece by piece.
優化用於 Claude（以產生更長的輸出）或 GPT-4。情境：這個提示的功能就如同行銷顧問的輸出。例如，它可能會輸出：「第一個月：發表部落格文章關於 X、Y；每日發推文分享小技巧；第二個月：LinkedIn 文章關於 Z；短影片介紹 Q…**」等，確保所有內容強化你的品牌敘事。這是一個高階策略，可以逐步執行。
    

    

      Competitive SWOT Coach: 
競爭性 SWOT 顧問：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “I am running [describe your business/startup]. Act as a business coach to conduct a quick SWOT analysis of my situation: list three strengths and three weaknesses internal to my business, and three opportunities and three threats from the market/external environment. Use what you know about similar businesses in this space (and assume typical challenges in [industry]). After the SWOT, suggest one strategic initiative I should focus on in the next quarter to leverage my strengths and opportunities or to mitigate a major weakness/threat.”
完整提示：「我正在經營[描述你的業務/新創公司]。請扮演一位業務顧問，為我進行快速的 SWOT 分析：列出三個與我的業務相關的內部優勢和三個內部弱點，以及三個來自市場/外部環境的機會和三個威脅。請運用你對此領域類似業務的了解（並假設該產業的典型挑戰）。在 SWOT 分析之後，建議我應該在下一季專注的一項戰略行動，以利用我的優勢和機會，或緩解一個主要的弱點/威脅。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Getting a strategic birds-eye view of where your business stands and what to prioritize without paying a consultant. 
使用情境：在不聘請顧問的情況下，獲得業務的戰略整體視野，並了解該 prioritise 什麼。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (GPT-4) or DeepSeek (if you want to incorporate real competitor data). 
      Example:
       The AI might identify an internal strength like an “agile product development team” and an external opportunity like “growing demand in Europe,” and then recommend an initiative such as expanding into a European market using fast product iterations. This prompt ensures you consider all facets (internal/external) in your strategy.
優化適用於 ChatGPT（GPT-4）或 DeepSeek（如果你想整合真實競爭對手資料）。例如：AI 可能會辨識出一個內部優勢如「靈活的產品開發團隊」，以及一個外部機會如「歐洲市場需求成長」，並建議採取如透過快速產品迭代拓展歐洲市場的行動。這個提示確保你在策略中考慮所有面向（內部/外部）。
    

    

      Communication & Professional Skills
溝通與專業技巧 
    

    

      Enhance your communication, leadership, and soft skills with prompts that coach you through writing and interaction challenges.
透過引導式提示，提升你的溝通、領導力與軟技能，協助你克服寫作與互動上的挑戰。
    

    

      Communication Style Translator: 
溝通風格翻譯者： 
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Assume the role of a communication style translator. I must send a message about [topic or issue] to [recipient/audience]. Draft it in three styles/tones: 1) formal and concise, 2) empathetic and supportive, and 3) persuasive and motivating. The core content should stay the same in each version. After each version, briefly note the key tone differences (e.g., word choice, sentence length, level of detail).”
完整提示：「假設你是一名溝通風格翻譯者。我必須針對[主題或議題]向[受眾或對象]發送訊息。請以三種風格/語調撰寫：1）正式且簡潔，2）同理心且支持性，3）說服力且鼓舞人心。每種版本的核心內容應保持一致。在每種版本後，簡要說明關鍵語調差異（例如：用詞選擇、句子長度、細節程度）。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Improving important emails or announcements by exploring different tones and choosing the most effective style for the situation. 
使用情境：透過探索不同的語氣，改善重要的電子郵件或公告，並選擇最適合情境的風格。 
    

    

      Optimized for
       GPT-4 (for subtle tone control) in ChatGPT. 
      Context:
       For example, this prompt can help a manager craft a delicate email to a team—one version might read very professionally, another more friendly, and another inspirational. Seeing all three allows the user to pick the approach that best fits their intent and the audience. It’s like having a communications coach instantly rewrite your message in multiple voices.
優化為適用 GPT-4（細膩語氣控制）的 ChatGPT 提示。情境：例如，這個提示可幫助經理撰寫一封給團隊的細膩電子郵件，一種版本可能非常專業，另一種則較為親切，還有一種具啟發性。看到這三種版本後，使用者可以選擇最符合其意圖和對象的溝通方式。這就像擁有即時的溝通顧問，能迅速以多種語調重寫你的訊息。
    

    

      Difficult Conversation Role-Play: 
困難對話角色扮演：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “I need to practice a difficult conversation. The scenario: [e.g., I have to give constructive criticism to an underperforming colleague]. Please role-play this with me. You will play [the colleague’s name] and respond realistically, possibly defensively or emotionally. I will start the dialogue by myself. Stay in character and have the colleague respond naturally. After a few exchanges, pause and give me feedback on how I handled it and improvement tips, then we can continue the role-play.”
完整提示：「我需要練習一場困難的對話。情境：[例如，我必須對表現不佳的同事給予具建設性的批評]。請與我進行角色扮演。你將扮演[同事的姓名]，並做出真實的回應，可能帶有防禦性或情緒化。我會先開始對話。請保持角色，讓同事自然回應。經過幾輪對話後，請暫停並給予我如何處理這場對話的反饋與改進建議，然後我們可以繼續角色扮演。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Practicing sensitive or high-stakes conversations (like performance reviews, salary negotiations, apologizing to a client, etc.) in a safe environment. 
使用情境：在安全的環境中練習敏感或高風險的對話（例如績效評估、薪資談判、向客戶道歉等）。 
    

    

      Optimized for
       Claude (for longer, memory-intensive dialogues) or GPT-4. 
      Example:
       The AI will simulate the person you need to talk to – allowing you to rehearse your wording and get comfortable responding to various reactions. This prompt provides the simulation and coaching feedback mid-way so you learn better phrasing or tactics. It’s akin to having an HR trainer or friend do a mock conversation with you, helping improve your confidence and communication skills.
針對 Claude（適合較長、記憶需求高的對話）或 GPT-4 優化。範例：AI 會模擬你必須與之對話的人，讓你練習用詞並適應各種反應。此提示在對話中段提供模擬與指導反饋，幫助你學習更好的表達方式或策略。這就如同有 HR 教練或朋友與你進行模擬對話，協助提升你的信心與溝通技巧。 
    

    

      Negotiation Tactics Coach: 
談判策略教練：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “You are an expert negotiation coach. I am a [profession, e.g., sales manager] who wants to improve my negotiation skills for [context, e.g., closing deals or salary discussions]. Give me a comprehensive guide covering how to prepare (research, setting goals), 3-4 effective negotiation techniques (with examples of phrasing), tips for reading the other party’s behavior, and strategies for handling impasses or difficult moments. Organize the advice into clear sections (Preparation, Techniques, Handling Objections, Closing the Deal).”
完整提示：「你是一位專業的談判教練。我是[職業，例如：銷售經理]，想要提升我的談判技巧用於[情境，例如：促成交易或薪資談判]。請為我提供一個全面的指南，涵蓋如何準備（研究、設定目標），3-4 種有效的談判技巧（包含語句範例），閱讀對方行為的技巧，以及處理僵局或困難時刻的策略。將建議分為明確的章節（準備、技巧、處理異議、結案）。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Learning or refining the negotiation skill in a structured way, as if reading a personalized handbook. 
使用情境：以結構化的方式學習或精進談判技巧，如同閱讀一份個人化手冊。
    

    

      Optimized for
       GPT-4 on ChatGPT (for detailed, structured output). 
      Context:
       The response will serve as a mini playbook on negotiation tailored to your role. For instance, it might include techniques like the “mirror and label” from FBI negotiators or the classic 
      BATNA
       (best alternative to a negotiated agreement) concept, all explained practically for your situation.
優化於 GPT-4 在 ChatGPT 上使用（以產生詳細、結構化的輸出）。情境：這個回應將作為一份為你量身打造的談判小手冊。例如，可能會包含 FBI 談判員使用的「鏡像與標籤」技巧，或經典的 BATNA（最佳替代協議）概念，並針對你的情境進行實用說明。
    

    

      This goes beyond generic tips by structuring the advice and making it actionable for your field.
這不僅僅是泛泛的建議，而是將建議結構化並使其針對你的領域具備可操作性。
    

    

      Mindset Shift Advisor: 
心態轉變顧問: 
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Act as a mindset coach. I often struggle with negative self-talk and self-doubt in my [work or personal life context]. Help me develop a more positive, growth-oriented mindset. Provide: a) 3 daily affirmations tailored to my situation that I can repeat, b) a suggestion for a short journaling exercise each evening to reframe negative thoughts from the day, and c) one practical exercise or habit I can do weekly to reinforce confidence and resilience (like a small risk or a challenge to overcome).”
完整提示 : 「請扮演心態教練。我常常在[工作或個人生活情境]中面臨負面自我對話與自我懷疑。幫助我培養更正面、成長導向的心態。請提供：a) 3 個適合我情境的每日肯定語，我可以重複使用，b) 每晚一個簡短的寫日記練習建議，用來重新詮釋當天的負面想法，以及 c) 一個我可以每周執行的實用練習或習慣，以強化自信與韌性（例如與我認為令人畏懼的人進行輕鬆對話）。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Improving one’s mindset and confidence over time with consistent practices is especially useful for professionals facing imposter syndrome or individuals working on personal growth. 
使用情境：透過持續的練習來改善心態與自信，對面臨冒名頂替綜合症的專業人士或正在進行個人成長的人來說尤其有幫助。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (GPT-4 or 3.5) or Claude. 
      Example:
       The AI might generate affirmations like 
      “I have the skills to overcome new challenges,”
       a journaling prompt to list two successes each day and what they say about your abilities, and a weekly exercise such as “Have a casual conversation with someone I find intimidating.” This prompt creates a mini coaching regimen to shift your thinking patterns towards growth and positivity.
優化適用於 ChatGPT（GPT-4 或 3.5）或 Claude。例如：AI 可能會產生如「我擁有克服新挑戰的技能」這樣的肯定語，寫日記提示可以列出當天的兩個成功事例以及這些事例說明了我具備哪些能力，而一個週期練習可能是「與我認為令人畏懼的人進行輕鬆對話」。這個提示創造了一個微型的教練計畫，用來轉變你的思考模式，朝向成長與正面思維。
    

    

      Learning Acceleration & Skill Mastery
學習加速與技能精通 
    

    

      Whether a student or a lifelong learner, these prompts help you learn faster and more deeply by tailoring the AI’s teaching style, generating study plans, and encouraging active engagement with the material.
無論是學生還是終身學習者，這些提示能幫助你更快、更深入地學習，透過調整 AI 的教學風格、生成學習計畫，並鼓勵你積極參與學習內容。 
    

    

      Complex Topic Explainer (Feynman Style): 
複雜主題解釋者（費曼風格）： 
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “I’m trying to learn [difficult topic]. Teach it to me in simple terms, as if I were 12 years old, using analogies or examples from everyday life. Then, I should identify gaps or common misunderstandings about this topic that I should watch out for. Finally, please give me a basic 2-week learning plan with daily sub-topics or exercises to gradually deepen my understanding of this topic. Include a suggestion for how to test myself (like a mini-quiz or a problem) at the end of each week.”
完整提示：「我正在學習[困難主題]。請用簡單的語言教我，就好像我還是 12 歲的孩童一樣，使用日常生活中類比或例子。然後，請指出我應該注意的知識缺口或常見誤解。最後，請為我提供一個基礎的 2 週學習計畫，包含每日的子主題或練習，以逐步深化我對這個主題的理解。每個週末請附上一個自我測試的建議（例如小測驗或問題）。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Quickly grasping a complex subject by breaking it down and then building a structured self-study approach. 
使用情境：透過拆解複雜主題，快速掌握並建立結構化的自學方法。
    

    

      Optimized for
       GPT-4 on ChatGPT (for clarity and depth) or Claude. 
      Context:
       This prompt combines the Feynman technique (explain in simple terms) with a learning schedule. For example, if the topic is quantum mechanics, the AI might use an analogy of a busy highway for electrons, warn you about a misconception (like confusing superposition with classical uncertainty), and then lay out a 14-day plan of concepts and readings. It ensures you get a simplified explanation and a path to learn the topic progressively.
最佳化於 GPT-4 在 ChatGPT（以清晰度和深度為考量）或 Claude。情境：這個提示結合費曼技巧（用簡單的語言解釋）與學習計畫。例如，如果主題是量子力學，AI 可能會用繁忙的高速公路來比喻電子，提醒你某個常見的誤解（如將疊加態與經典的不確定性混淆），然後列出一個 14 天的概念與閱讀計畫。這確保你獲得簡化的解釋，並有一個逐步學習該主題的路徑。
    

    

      Focused Skill Breakdown & Practice Plan: 
專注技能拆解與練習計畫：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Design a deliberate practice routine for me to improve [a specific skill]. First, break down [the skill] into its core sub-skills or components. For each sub-skill, suggest a targeted exercise or drill that I can do regularly. Then, outline a 4-week practice schedule, specifying which exercises to do on which days (with rest or review days as needed). Also, include a way to track progress or measure improvement each week.”
完整提示：「為我設計一個刻意練習計畫，以提升 [特定技能]。首先，將 [該技能] 拆解為其核心子技能或組成部分。針對每個子技能，建議一個可以定期進行的專項練習或訓練。然後，列出一個 4 週的練習計畫，說明每個日子該進行哪些練習（必要時包含休息或複習日）。同時，包含一種方式，用以每週追蹤進度或衡量進步。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Mastering a professional or personal skill (e.g., coding, public speaking, playing guitar) efficiently by focusing on its building blocks. 
使用情境：有效掌握專業或個人技能（例如程式設計、公開演講、彈吉他）的方法，透過專注於其基本組成部分。 
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT or Claude. 
      Example:
       For learning an instrument, the AI might break down guitar playing into chord transitions, strumming, and scales, then assign daily exercises for each. It could suggest 
      “Week 1: basic chords practice 15 min, strumming patterns 10 min… Week 4: combine chords and strumming in a simple song”
      , along with a progress metric like increasing tempo or reducing errors. This prompt yields a highly actionable training plan rather than generic advice.
針對 ChatGPT 或 Claude 優化。例如：在學習樂器時，AI 可能會將吉他演奏分解為和弦轉換、撥弦模式與音階，並為每一部分安排每日練習。它可能會建議「第一週：基本和弦練習 15 分鐘，撥弦模式 10 分鐘… 第四週：將和弦與撥弦模式結合在一首簡單的歌曲中」，並搭配進度指標，如提高節奏或減少錯誤。此提示能產生高度可執行的訓練計畫，而非泛泛的建議。 
    

    

      High-Impact 80/20 Learning Planner: 
高效益 80/20 學習計畫：
    

    

      Full Prompt:
       
      “I want to learn 
      [broad topic or skill]
       faster. As an 80/20 learning expert, identify the 20% of sub-topics or techniques within 
      [the topic]
       that will give me 80% of the practical value. Explain why these are high-impact. Then, create a focused learning plan prioritizing these key areas first. The plan should include recommended resources or methods for each high-impact area and suggestions to avoid lesser important details initially. Present it as a prioritized list of what to learn (most important to least), with brief study tips for each.”
我想更快地學習[broad topic or skill]。作為一位 80/20 學習專家，請識別出[主題]中佔 20%的子主題或技巧，這些內容將為我帶來 80%的實用價值。說明為何這些是高影響力的重點。然後，為我制定一個專注的學習計畫，優先處理這些關鍵領域。計畫應包含每個高影響力領域的推薦資源或方法，並建議在初期避免處理較不重要的細節。請以由最重要到最不重要的順序，呈現一個優先級清單，並為每個項目提供簡短的學習提示。 
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Quickly ramping up in a new subject by focusing on the most valuable parts (great for busy students or when picking up a skill under time constraints). 
使用情境：透過專注於最有價值的部分，快速掌握新主題（非常適合忙碌的學生或在時間有限的情況下學習新技能）。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (GPT-4 for thoughtful selection) or Claude. 
      Context:
       For example, if the topic is learning a language for business travel, the AI might identify that mastering the 500 most common words and basic sentence structure yields 80% understanding, whereas complex grammar yields less initial payoff. It would then prioritize vocabulary and common phrases, provide resources like flashcards or apps, and de-prioritize literary tenses. This prompt makes the AI apply the Pareto Principle to your learning, accelerating your progress.
優化為適用於 ChatGPT（GPT-4 用於深入選擇）或 Claude。情境：例如，如果主題是為商務旅行學習語言，AI 可能會識別出掌握 500 個最常見的單字和基本句型可以達到 80%的理解，而複雜語法則在初期效益較低。它會優先處理單字和常用短語，提供如閃卡或 APP 等學習資源，並降低對文學時態的優先級。這個提示讓 AI 將帕累托原則應用在你的學習上，加速你的進步。
    

    

      Comprehension Quizmaster: 
理解測驗大師：
    

    

      Full Prompt
      :
       
      “Help me study [subject or book] by quizzing me. First, ask me five multiple-choice questions covering the important points of [the material]. Please wait for my answers. For each answer I give, please tell me if it’s correct and provide a brief explanation or the correct answer if I was wrong. Make the questions thought-provoking rather than trivial details. After the quiz, based on my performance, give me a short recommendation on topics to review further.”
完整提示：「幫助我學習[主題或書籍]，透過測驗我來進行。首先，請問五個選擇題，涵蓋[內容]的重要重點。請等我回答。對於我每一個回答，請告訴我是否正確，並提供簡短的解釋或正確答案（如果我答錯了）。請讓問題具有啟發性，而非瑣碎細節。測驗結束後，根據我的表現，給我一個短暫的建議，指出需要進一步複習的主題。」
       
    

    

      Use Case:
       Engaging in active recall and self-testing, which is proven to boost learning (more effective than passive reading). 
使用情境：進行主動回憶與自我測試，這已被證明能提升學習效果（比被動閱讀更有效）。
    

    

      Optimized for
       ChatGPT (ideal in an interactive session) or Claude. 
      Example:
       This turns the AI into a custom exam reviewer. If you’ve just read a chapter on marketing strategy, the AI might ask, 
      “Which of the following best describes the concept of ‘segmentation’? A, B, C, or D?”
       and so on. It then explains the answers. The prompt essentially creates a dynamic study session, pinpointing your weak spots. It’s a lesser-known way to use ChatGPT as a tutor that adapts to you – far more engaging than flashcards and not commonly found in essential prompt lists.
優化用於 ChatGPT（適合互動式會話）或 Claude。例如：這會將 AI 轉化為自訂的考試評分者。如果你剛剛讀完一章關於行銷策略的內容，AI 可能會問：「以下哪一個選項最能描述『市場區隔』的概念？A、B、C 或 D？」等等，並說明答案。這個提示基本上創造了一個動態的學習會話，能準確指出你的弱點。這是一種較少被提及的使用 ChatGPT 作為導師的方式，能根據你的需求進行調整——遠比閃卡更有趣，也不常見於基本提示清單中。
    

    

      These prompts are novel and actionable, originating from cutting-edge users and prompt engineers rather than generic guides. By categorizing them into personal systems, decision-making, ADHD hacks, executive strategy, communication, and accelerated learning, you can easily find a prompt to boost whatever aspect of productivity or effectiveness you need. Feel free to customize the placeholders (in [brackets]) to fit your situation, and choose the AI tool best suited for the job (ChatGPT for general use, Claude for lengthy or conversational tasks, DeepSeek for real-time research integration, etc.). These community-tested prompts can function like your personal playbook, helping you leverage AI as a powerful ally in entrepreneurship, studies, and everyday productivity.
這些提示是創新且具實用性的，來自於先鋒用戶與提示工程師，而非一般的指南。透過將它們分類為個人系統、決策制定、ADHD 技巧、執行策略、溝通以及加速學習，您可以輕鬆找到適合提升您所需生產力或效率方面的提示。請自由地根據您的情況調整括號中的佔位符，並選擇最適合該任務的 AI 工具（如一般用途使用 ChatGPT、長篇或對話型任務使用 Claude、即時研究整合使用 DeepSeek 等）。這些經過社群測試的提示可以像您的個人戰術手冊一樣運作，幫助您將 AI 視為創業、學習和日常生產力的強大盟友。
    

    

      Novel and Creative ChatGPT Use Cases Across Domains
跨領域的創新與創意 ChatGPT 使用案例 
    

    

      Art & Literature 
      🌟
藝術與文學 🌟 
    

    

      ChatGPT has been leveraged as a creative partner in storytelling, poetry, music, and art in striking ways. Here are some unique examples:
ChatGPT 已以驚人的方式被用作故事創作、詩歌、音樂與藝術的創意夥伴。以下是一些獨特的範例：
    

    

      AI-assisted Novel Writing
       – 
AI 輔助小說創作 – 
    

    

      In Japan, author Rie Kudan openly admitted that about 5% of her award-winning novel 
      Tokyo-to Dojo-to
       was written by ChatGPT. After winning the prestigious Akutagawa Prize, she explained that she “made full use” of generative AI to craft portions of the text.​  
在日本，作家久田莉音公開承認，她獲獎的小說《東京與道場》約有 5%的內容是由 ChatGPT 所寫。在獲得聲譽卓著的角川賞後，她解釋說她「充分運用」生成式 AI 來撰寫部分文字。​
    

    

      This hybrid approach showcases how human writers can weave AI-generated passages into literature in novel ways. Similarly, science-fiction writer Tim Boucher used ChatGPT (along with image AI) to mass-produce short “AI Lore” books – nearly 100 illustrated sci-fi ebooks in under a year​.
這種混合方式展現了人類作家如何以創新方式將 AI 生成的段落融入文學作品中。同樣地，科幻作家 Tim Boucher 使用 ChatGPT（搭配圖像 AI）大量生產短篇「AI 神話」書籍 – 在不到一年的時間內，幾乎生產了 100 本插圖科幻電子書。​
    

    

      
        

        Each book was 2,000–5,000 words with dozens of AI-generated images, allowing an unprecedented rapid creative output. Boucher’s experiment demonstrates how AI can turbocharge literary production and world-building.
      
每本書約有 2,000 至 5,000 字，並包含數十張 AI 生成的圖片，這使得創意產出的速度前所未有的快速。Boucher 的實驗說明了 AI 如何加速文學創作與世界觀的建立。
    

    

      Unique Poetry & Lyrics
       – 
獨特的詩歌與歌詞 – 
    

    

      
    

    

      Writers and hobbyists have pushed ChatGPT into poetic territory, often with surprising results. For example, one user prompted ChatGPT to rap about “the future of meat”, yielding a humorous rap complete with verses, a bridge, and a catchy (if clunky) chorus about alternative protein​.
作家與愛好者已將 ChatGPT 推進詩歌領域，常常產生令人驚訝的結果。例如，有位使用者提示 ChatGPT 以「肉類的未來」為題進行說唱，結果得到一首幽默的說唱作品，包含段落、橋段與一個（雖然有些笨拙）朗朗上口的副歌。
    

    

      
        

        While it wasn’t exactly Grammy-worthy, it proved AI can generate song lyrics on quirky topics. Others have had ChatGPT write poetry in specific styles or even mimic iconic poems for fun​.
        
雖然這首作品並非獲得格萊美獎的等級，但它證明了 AI 有能力在一些奇特主題上創作歌曲歌詞。其他人則讓 ChatGPT 以特定風格寫詩，甚至為了娛樂而模仿經典詩作。

        

        The AI’s ability to pastiche styles means you can get, say, a Shakespearean sonnet about quantum physics or a haiku in the voice of a famous poet. The results might need polish, but they provide a fresh wellspring of creative inspiration for human poets and lyricists.
      
AI 具備模仿不同風格的能力，這意味著你可以得到一首關於量子物理的莎士比亞十四行詩，或是一首以著名詩人聲調寫成的俳句。雖然結果可能需要一些潤飾，但它為人類詩人與歌詞作家提供了新的創意靈感來源。
    

    

      
    

    

      Music Composition Experiments
       – 
音樂創作實驗 – 
    

    

      
    

    

      Musicians have tapped ChatGPT for help composing music and songs in text form. One creative approach was asking ChatGPT to output melodies in ABC notation (a text-based music notation). A user had ChatGPT generate an “emotional sci-fi theme” and even a Eurovision-style song in ABC format, then converted these to MIDI audio. 
音樂人已開始利用 ChatGPT 協助以文字形式進行音樂與歌曲的創作。其中一種創意方式是請 ChatGPT 產生以 ABC 記譜法（一種文字形式的音樂記譜）表示的旋律。有使用者讓 ChatGPT 產生一首「情感科幻主題曲」，甚至以 Eurovision 風格的歌曲形式撰寫 ABC 記譜，再轉換為 MIDI 音訊。
    

    

      Amazingly, ChatGPT managed to produce coherent tunes that, when rendered, carried the requested style. This shows AI’s potential beyond prose – assisting in music creation by suggesting chords, melodies or song structures via text. It’s like having a super flexible session musician who speaks in code.
令人驚訝的是，ChatGPT 能夠產生合邏輯的旋律，當轉譯成音訊後，還能呈現出所要求的風格。這顯示出 AI 的潛力不僅限於文字創作，也能透過文字建議和諧、旋律或歌曲結構，協助音樂創作。就像是擁有了一位超靈活的現場樂手，只會用代碼說話。 
    

    

      
    

    

      Science & Tech 
      🔬🤖
科學與科技 🔬🤖
    

    

      Beyond the arts, people have found extraordinary uses for ChatGPT in scientific research, coding, and tech innovation. These go far beyond writing assistance – using the AI in unconventional, problem-solving roles:
在藝術領域之外，人們也發現 ChatGPT 在科學研究、程式設計和科技創新方面有著非凡的應用。這些應用遠遠超出了寫作輔助的範疇，將 AI 用在非傳統的、解決問題的角色上：
    

    

      Biology & Medicine – 
生物與醫學 –
    

    

      Some scientists have applied ChatGPT’s underlying language models to genomics and health data. In one experiment, biologists used GPT models to identify pathogen mutations​. 
一些科學家已經將 ChatGPT 的基礎語言模型應用於基因組學和健康數據分析。在一個實驗中，生物學家使用 GPT 模型來識別病原體的變異。
    

    

      By feeding genetic data to a GPT-based system, they could have it highlight unusual mutations in a virus’s genome. This novel approach treats DNA sequences a bit like language, leveraging AI to spot patterns that human experts might miss. It’s an emerging technique that hints at AI’s potential in disease research and bioinformatics. (Of course, any such findings still need human verification, but it’s a creative assistive tool.)
透過將遺傳數據輸入基於 GPT 的系統，他們可以讓系統標註病毒基因組中不尋常的變異。這種新穎的方法將 DNA 序列視為一種語言，利用 AI 來發現人類專家可能忽略的模式。這是一種正在興起的技術，預示了 AI 在疾病研究和生物資訊學方面的潛力。（當然，任何這樣的發現仍需人類驗證，但它是一種創新的輔助工具。）
    

    

      Chemistry Lab Assistant
       – 
化學實驗室助理 – 
    

    

      In a groundbreaking project at Carnegie Mellon University, researchers augmented GPT-4 with chemistry knowledge and hooked it up to a robotic lab. The enhanced ChatGPT was given the interface to a remote chemistry lab stocked with liquid handlers and analysis tools. When asked to synthesize a target compound, the AI could 
      plan an experiment and issue commands to the lab robots
       to mix chemicals and run reactions​. 
在卡內基梅隆大學一項突破性的專案中，研究人員將化學知識加入 GPT-4，並連接至一個機械化實驗室。升級後的 ChatGPT 被賦予遠端化學實驗室的介面，該實驗室配備液體處理裝置與分析工具。當被要求合成目標化合物時，AI 可以規劃實驗並發出指令給實驗室機械人，混合化學物質並執行反應​。 
    

    

      In other words, ChatGPT effectively acted as a chemistry researcher, devising and executing an experiment in real-time. This “ChemGPT” successfully produced the desired chemical compounds​. 
換言之，ChatGPT 有效地扮演化學研究者的角色，即時規劃並執行實驗。這個「ChemGPT」成功製造出所需的化學化合物​。 
    

    

      Such a use is highly novel – it suggests future AIs might help scientists by autonomously carrying out routine experiments or searching for new chemical reactions, vastly speeding up R&D in science.
這種應用極具創新性 – 它暗示未來的 AI 可能協助科學家，自動執行常規實驗或尋找新的化學反應，大幅加速科學研究與開發。
    

    

      Space & Data Analysis
       – 
太空與資料分析 – 
    

    

      Even NASA has gotten in on the action. The space agency has been exploring GPT-based tools to help analyze spacecraft telemetry and data​. 
連美國國家航空暨太空總署（NASA）也加入了這股風潮。這間太空機構正在探討基於 GPT 的工具，以協助分析太空船的 telemetry（ telemetry 是指遠端測量與傳輸的資料）與資料。
    

    

      Instead of manually combing through sensor readings, engineers can have an AI system flag anomalies or summarize mission data in plain language. ChatGPT’s knack for understanding context means it could parse streams of technical data and highlight what’s important. This is an unconventional use of a chatbot – essentially as a smart data analyst for astronomy and spaceflight. 
工程師們不再需要手動翻閱感測器讀數，而是可以讓 AI 系統標記異常或以自然語言總結任務資料。ChatGPT 擅長理解上下文，因此可以解析技術資料流並突出重點。這是一種非傳統的聊天機器人應用方式，基本上就如同為天文學與太空飛行打造的智能資料分析師。
    

    

      While still experimental, it shows promise in making sense of the massive data sets that modern science accumulates. (Outside of NASA, many researchers are also using ChatGPT to summarize scientific papers, brainstorm hypotheses, or even draft sections of research papers​ – though always with human oversight due to AI’s inaccuracies.)
雖然仍處於實驗階段，但這顯示出在處理現代科學所累積的龐大資料集方面，具有很大的潛力。(除了 NASA 之外，許多研究人員也正在使用 ChatGPT 來總結科學論文、激發假說，甚至撰寫論文的部分內容 – 然而，總是會有研究人員進行人工監督，以修正 AI 的不準確之處。)
    

    

      Coding and Engineering Creativity
       – 
程式設計與工程創意 – 
    

    

      Developers have embraced ChatGPT as an AI pair programmer, and some have pushed it in wild directions. There are reports of programmers using ChatGPT to create entire small apps or games from scratch, just by iteratively prompting for code and debugging. In one quirky case, an engineer even got ChatGPT to simulate a whole Linux computer within the chat – treating the AI like a virtual machine. By instructing “Act as a Linux terminal,” users interacted with ChatGPT as if it were an operating system: they ran commands, created files, and it responded with simulated outputs accordingly​. 
開發者已經將 ChatGPT 擁抱為一種 AI 對程式設計師，有些人甚至將其推向極端的應用方向。有報導指出，有些程式設計師僅透過反覆提示產生程式碼與除錯，就用 ChatGPT 創造出完整的微型應用程式或遊戲。在一則有趣的案例中，一位工程師甚至讓 ChatGPT 模擬出一整台 Linux 電腦，將 AI 視為一種虛擬機器。透過指示「請以 Linux 終端機的身分作答」，使用者便能與 ChatGPT 互動，彷彿它就是一個作業系統：他們執行指令、建立檔案，而 ChatGPT 也會根據這些操作模擬出相應的輸出結果。
    

    

      The chatbot “understood” the filesystem and could even execute code logic internally, demonstrating an unexpected emergent capability. This fun experiment shows how far AI’s 
      knowledge imitation
       can go – ChatGPT had absorbed so much tech info that it could mimic an entire OS environment​. 
這款聊天機器人「理解」了檔案系統，甚至能內部執行程式邏輯，展現出一種令人驚訝的突發能力。這個有趣的實驗說明了 AI 在知識模仿方面能走多遠 – ChatGPT 吸收了如此多的科技資訊，竟可以模擬出整個作業系統的環境。
    

    

      On a more practical note, developers also use ChatGPT to generate algorithm ideas, refactor legacy code, write documentation, and even design new software by conversing about architecture. These inventive uses in tech hint at a future where AI is a collaborator in engineering and discovery, not just a tool for answering questions.
在實務應用方面，開發者也使用 ChatGPT 來產生演算法構思、重構舊有程式碼、撰寫文件，甚至透過討論架構來設計新軟體。這些在科技領域的創新應用，預示著一個未來，其中 AI 將成為工程與發現的夥伴，而不僅只是回答問題的工具。
    

    

      Business & Productivity 
      💼⚙️
商業與生產力 💼⚙️ 
    

    

      In the business world, ChatGPT’s creativity and efficiency gains are being harnessed in ways beyond the usual email drafting. Entrepreneurs, marketers, and companies have cooked up some clever uses:
在商業界，ChatGPT 的創造力與效率提升正被用在超越一般電子郵件撰寫的領域。創業者、市場營銷人員與企業已經想出一些聰明的應用方式：
    

    

      Marketing Content & Copywriting at Scale
       – 
大規模的市場營銷內容與文案撰寫 –
    

    

      Many businesses face the grind of churning out content (product descriptions, ads, social posts). ChatGPT has emerged as a game-changer here. For example, an online fashion retailer used ChatGPT to generate engaging product descriptions for its ever-changing inventory​.
許多企業面臨持續產生內容（產品說明、廣告、社交媒體貼文）的壓力。ChatGPT 在這方面成為了改變遊戲規則的工具。例如，一家線上服飾零售商利用 ChatGPT 來生成吸引人的產品說明，以應對其不斷變動的庫存。
    

    

      By feeding the AI details like material, style, and brand voice, they let it draft hundreds of unique descriptions in a fraction of the time a human team would take. The result was not only faster content creation but also more consistent, on-brand copy across the site – and it even boosted conversion rates due to the improved wording​.
透過輸入 AI 材質、風格和品牌語調等細節，他們讓 AI 能在極短的時間內撰寫出數百個獨特的說明文字。結果不僅加快了內容創作的速度，也讓網站上的說明文字更加一致且符合品牌形象，甚至因為語詞的改善而提升了轉化率。
    

    

      In another case, a fitness brand automated its social media posts and replies using ChatGPT’s tone-mimicking abilities​. The AI could draft upbeat captions, craft replies to common comments, and keep the conversation flowing with followers, freeing up the human marketing team to focus on strategy. These are not your run-of-the-mill uses – they show ChatGPT acting as a junior copywriter or community manager, handling the repetitive writing tasks so humans can concentrate on creative strategy.
另一個案例中，一家健身品牌利用 ChatGPT 的語氣模擬功能自動化其社交媒體貼文與回覆。AI 可以撰寫活潑的標語、回應常見評論，並與追蹤者持續互動，讓人類的行銷團隊得以專注於策略制定。這些並非普通的應用方式 – 它們顯示了 ChatGPT 像是擔任助理文案撰寫者或社群管理員的角色，處理重複的寫作任務，讓人類專注於創意策略。
    

    

      Idea Generation & Strategy
       – 
點子產生與策略 –
    

    

      Businesses have also used ChatGPT as an “ideation” engine for brainstorming products and strategies. Wharton professor Ethan Mollick famously dubbed ChatGPT his “AI co-founder” and demonstrated how it can help aspiring entrepreneurs. He prompted ChatGPT to propose dozens of tailored startup ideas for different niches and personal backgrounds – and found that many ideas were surprisingly viable​. 
企業也將 ChatGPT 用作「創意發想」引擎，用於產品與策略的腦力激盪。沃頓商學院教授 Ethan Mollick 著名地將 ChatGPT 称為他的「AI 合夥人」，並展示它如何協助有志創業者。他提示 ChatGPT 提出數十種針對不同細分市場與個人背景的創業點子 – 並發現許多點子出乎意料地可行​。 
    

    

      Founders are using ChatGPT to generate business plans, suggest marketing angles, and even conduct SWOT analyses. For instance, you can ask it for “10 viral marketing stunt ideas for a new eco-friendly sneaker” and get back a list of creative concepts to build on. One marketing agency described how they turned two hours of ChatGPT prompting into a month-long content plan, using the AI to map out blog topics, social media themes, and campaign schedules​. 
創辦人使用 ChatGPT 來制定商業計畫、建議行銷角度，甚至進行 SWOT 分析。例如，你可以詢問「為新推出的環保運動鞋提出 10 個能造成病毒式傳播的行銷活動點子」，並得到一連串創意概念來作為發展基礎。有一家行銷機構說明他們如何透過兩小時的 ChatGPT 提示，製作出一個月的內容計畫，利用 AI 來規劃部落格主題、社交媒體趨勢與行銷活動排期​。 
    

    

      By acting as a supercharged brainstorming partner, ChatGPT helps teams move faster from blank page to actionable plan. It’s like having a consultant on call 24/7 to bounce ideas off – though the best results come when you review and refine the AI’s suggestions with human judgment.
透過作為一個強化版的腦力激盪夥伴，ChatGPT 帮助團隊更快地從空白頁轉化為可執行的計畫。就像是隨時隨地都有諮詢師可以提供建議，不過最好的結果往往來自於你以人類的判斷力來審閱與調整 AI 的建議。
    

    

      Creative Campaigns & Customer Engagement
       – 
創意行銷方案與顧客互動 –
    

    

      Some companies have gone a step further, integrating ChatGPT into public-facing campaigns. A standout example is Coca-Cola’s “Create Real Magic” campaign in 2023. Coca-Cola built an online platform that let users generate art and slogans using a combo of DALL-E 2 for images and ChatGPT for text​. 
有些公司更進一步，將 ChatGPT 整合至面對公眾的行銷活動中。一個突出的例子是可口可樂 2023 年的「Create Real Magic」活動。可口可樂建立了一個線上平台，讓用戶透過 DALL-E 2 生成圖片與 ChatGPT 產生文字，來創造藝術作品與標語。
    

    

      Fans could enter prompts, and the AI would help create custom visuals 
      and taglines
      , blending the Coca-Cola brand with user input. The campaign yielded over 120,000 pieces of user-generated content and kept visitors engaged on the site for minutes at a time​. 
粉絲可以輸入提示，AI 會協助產生客製化的視覺與標語，將可口可樂的品牌與用戶的輸入融合。這項活動產生了超過 12 萬件用戶自創內容，並讓訪客每次在網站上停留數分鐘。
    

    

      This was a fresh way to involve consumers – essentially crowdsourcing marketing content with AI as the facilitator. 
這是一種新穎的方式來參與消費者，簡而言之就是以 AI 為媒介，進行行銷內容的集體創作。
    

    

      On a smaller scale, businesses have used ChatGPT to power chatbots that interact with customers in a fun, personable way (for example, a pizza chain letting a ChatGPT-based bot banter with users as they build their dream pizza). 
在較小規模上，企業也運用 ChatGPT 來驅動聊天機器人，以有趣且親切的方式與顧客互動（例如，一家披薩連鎖店讓基於 ChatGPT 的機器人與用戶閒聊，協助他們打造夢想披薩）。
    

    

      By leveraging ChatGPT’s conversational flair, brands create interactive experiences that stand out. It’s not just about efficiency; it’s about doing something novel that gets people talking and sharing.
善用 ChatGPT 的對話魅力，品牌能創造出令人印象深刻的互動體驗。這不只是關於效率，而是做些新穎的事情，讓人們願意討論與分享。
    

    

      Automation & Efficiency Hacks
       –
自動化與效率技巧 –
    

    

       Office workers and startups alike are finding offbeat ways to automate drudgery with ChatGPT. There are reports of teams automating their customer support by connecting ChatGPT to email or chat systems to draft first responses to common inquiries, which human staff then quickly review and send. Some have integrated ChatGPT with project management tools – for instance, auto-generating task lists or meeting summaries. 
辦公室工作者與新創公司 alike 都發現了用 ChatGPT 來自動化繁重工作的獨特方式。有報導指出，一些團隊透過將 ChatGPT 連結至電子郵件或聊天系統，自動撰寫常見問題的首輪回應，再由人工作業人員快速審閱後發送。有些人則將 ChatGPT 整合至專案管理工具中，例如自動產生任務清單或會議摘要。
    

    

      In one humorous case, a person even used ChatGPT to write gentle rejection letters for all the job applications they didn’t want to pursue, customizing each note politely in seconds. 
有一個幽默的案例，有人甚至使用 ChatGPT 來撰寫溫和的拒絕信，用以回應那些他們不感興趣的工作申請，並在幾秒內客製化每一封信件，保持禮貌的語氣。
    

    

      While these uses aren’t headline-making, they show a creative mindset toward productivity: whenever there’s a repetitive writing or ideation task, see if ChatGPT can handle the heavy lifting. 
雖然這些應用未必是新聞熱點，但它們展現出一種創意的生產力思維： whenever 有重複的寫作或構思任務，就看看 ChatGPT 是否能承擔主要工作。
    

    

      The result is often a significant time saver, letting people focus on decision-making and execution. As long as the outputs are checked for accuracy, this kind of AI-driven automation can streamline workflows in pretty much any business domain.
結果往往能節省大量時間，讓人們專注於決策與執行。只要確認輸出的準確性，這種由 AI 帶動的自動化就能在幾乎任何商業領域中簡化工作流程。
    

    

      Fun & Experimental 
      🎲🎉
有趣 & 創意實驗 🎲🎉 
    

    

      Finally, some of the most delightfully creative ChatGPT uses come from tinkerers and hobbyists exploring its limits for entertainment or personal projects. These often yield surprising and hilarious results:
最後，一些最令人驚喜的 ChatGPT 應用來自於愛好者與實驗者，他們為了娛樂或個人專案而探索其極限。這些應用常常產生令人驚訝且好笑的結果：
    

    

      AI Dungeon Master & Storyteller
       – 
    

    

      ChatGPT can improvise stories on the fly, which makes it a perfect Dungeon Master for Dungeons & Dragons or other role-playing games. People have run entire D&D sessions with ChatGPT-4 as the DM, guiding players through adventures. One dad described playing D&D with his kids where ChatGPT dished out a fantastical quest – and it was amazingly responsive to their wild ideas​.
ChatGPT 可以即時編織故事，這使得它成為 Dungeons & Dragons 或其他角色扮演遊戲的完美 Dungeon Master。有人曾用 ChatGPT-4 作為 DM，帶領玩家進行完整的 D&D 會話，引導他們經歷冒險。一位爸爸描述他與孩子們一起玩 D&D 的經歷，其中 ChatGPT 賦予了一個奇幻的任務，而且對他們天馬行空的想法反應驚人​。 
    

    

      At one point, the players decided to 
      befriend
       a group of zombies by pitching a multi-level marketing scheme to them (yes, really). Instead of balking, the AI DM rolled with it: it narrated how the undead actually considered the pyramid scheme and agreed to give it a try, defusing the combat encounter in a comical way​. 
有一次，玩家決定與一群殭屍建立友誼，並向它們推銷多層次行銷計畫（是的，真的有這回事）。AI DM 没有退縮，反而順勢而為：它敘述了這些無魂之軀實際上考慮了金字塔式行銷模式，並答應嘗試一下，以一種喜劇的方式化解了戰鬥場景​。 
    

    

      This absurd scenario shows how flexible and imaginative ChatGPT can be in an open-ended narrative game. It keeps the story going no matter what curveball the players throw, from negotiating with monsters to exploring offbeat side quests. 
這個荒謬的情節展現了 ChatGPT 在開放式敘事遊戲中多麼靈活且富有創意。不管玩家投擲什麼出人意料的變數，從與怪物談判到探索離奇的支线任务，它都能讓故事持續進行。
    

    

      Beyond D&D, users have enjoyed text adventures and interactive fiction where ChatGPT essentially becomes a collaborative storytelling partner, making up characters, dialogue, and plot twists in real time. Every play-through is unique, limited only by your imagination (and maybe the AI’s content guidelines).
除了 D&D 之外，使用者也享受過文字冒險與互動小說，其中 ChatGPT 幾乎成為一個協同敘事的夥伴，即時創造角色、對話與情節轉折。每一次的遊玩都是獨一無二的，僅受限於你的想像力（以及可能的 AI 內容準則）。
    

    

      Simulating Unlikely Things
       – 
模擬不可能的事物 –
    

    

      Users love to poke at ChatGPT’s ability to pretend to be other systems or entities. One famous experiment had people convincing ChatGPT to act like a fully functional 
      Linux computer
      . With a cleverly crafted prompt, the AI was asked to behave as a Linux terminal – and it succeeded to a shocking degree​. 
使用者喜歡挑戰 ChatGPT 模擬其他系統或實體的能力。有一個著名的實驗，人們成功說服 ChatGPT 扮演一台完整的 Linux 電腦。透過巧妙設計的提示，AI 被要求表現為 Linux 終端機 – 並以驚人程度達成目標。
    

    

      The user could type commands like 
      ls
       or 
      pwd
       and ChatGPT would output a pretend directory listing or present a file system prompt, as if you were actually on a Unix machine. It could even execute code in this simulated environment (for example, running a Python snippet and returning the result)​. 
使用者可以輸入像是 ls 或 pwd 這樣的指令，ChatGPT 會輸出虛構的目錄清單或顯示檔案系統提示，彷彿你真的在使用 Unix 機器。它甚至可以在這個模擬環境中執行程式碼（例如運行一個 Python 片段並回傳結果）。
    

    

      Of course, no real code was running – ChatGPT was just very convincingly imitating how a computer would respond, based on what it learned from documentation and forums. Similarly, others have prompted ChatGPT to masquerade as historical figures, to speak in pirate slang, or even to emulate an old-school text adventure engine. 
當然，並沒有真正的程式在執行 – ChatGPT 只是非常逼真地模擬電腦會如何回應，根據它從文件和論壇中學習到的內容。同樣地，其他人也提示 ChatGPT 假裝成歷史人物、用海盜俚語對話，甚至模擬舊式文字冒險遊戲引擎。
    

    

      These playful uses reveal the model’s chameleon-like quality: if you ask it to stay in character (whether that’s “wise medieval wizard” or “Linux OS”), it will do its best to comply, creating the illusion of a whole new persona or system living inside the chat. It’s both entertaining and a bit mind-bending to see an AI 
      method-act
       like this.
這些有趣的應用展現了模型的變色龍特質：如果你要求它保持角色（不管是「智慧的中世紀巫師」還是「Linux 作業系統」），它會盡力配合，創造出一種全新的個性或系統的幻覺。看到 AI 如此投入地演出，既有趣又稍顯令人驚訝。
    

    

      Puzzle Master & Game Designer
       – 
解謎大師 & 遊戲設計師 –
    

    

      ChatGPT’s creativity isn’t limited to text and dialogue – it can generate games and puzzles too. People have used it to invent new riddles, brain teasers, and trivia quizzes on the spot. For instance, you can prompt ChatGPT: “Give me a murder mystery riddle” or “Create a logic puzzle about a secret society,” and it will oblige with a full puzzle (and usually the answer, hidden or at the end)​. 
ChatGPT 的創造力不僅限於文字和對話 – 它也能產生遊戲和謎題。人們已經用它即興發明新的謎語、腦筋急轉彎和 trivia 測驗。例如，你可以提示 ChatGPT：「給我一個謀殺謎語」或「創造一個關於秘密組織的邏輯謎題」，它就會提供完整的謎題（通常還會附上答案，藏在謎題末尾）。
    

    

      This has led some to use ChatGPT as a party trick or educational tool, providing endless puzzles to solve. In the classroom, teachers have experimented with ChatGPT to create 
      escape-room style
       challenges for students, complete with clues and codes to crack​. 
這讓一些人將 ChatGPT 用作一種把戲或教育工具，提供無限的謎題讓學生解決。在課堂上，老師們已經嘗試用 ChatGPT 來設計類似逃脫遊戲的挑戰，並附有線索和密碼等元素​。
    

    

      On the game design front, hobbyist programmers have paired ChatGPT with other tools to make simple text games. One Reddit user even made an “infinitely replayable” escape room game where ChatGPT generates the room description, puzzles, and solutions dynamically each playthrough (ensuring you can’t spoil the game by searching for answers)​
在遊戲設計方面，業餘程式設計師們將 ChatGPT 與其他工具結合，製作出簡單的文字遊戲。有位 Reddit 使用者甚至製作了一款「無限重玩」的逃脫遊戲，ChatGPT 會在每次遊玩時動態生成房間描述、謎題與解答（確保你無法透過搜尋答案來破壞遊戲體驗）​。
    

    

      It’s a testament to AI’s generative flexibility that it can whip up a puzzle or mini-game tailored to your prompts. For pure fun, some users ask ChatGPT to 
      play games like 20 Questions, act as a trivia host, or simulate a “choose your own adventure” story
      , turning a simple chat into interactive entertainment.
這正是 AI 生成靈活性的見證，它能根據你的提示快速製作出專屬的謎題或小遊戲。為了純粹的娛樂，一些使用者會請 ChatGPT 玩 20 個問題這樣的遊戲，或擔任 trivia 主持人，甚至模擬「選擇你的冒險」故事，將一場簡單的對話轉化為互動娛樂。
    

    

      Quirky Personal Uses
       – 
奇特的個人用途 –
    

    

      Finally, there are all the uncategorizable, personal ways people have enjoyed ChatGPT. 
最後，還有許多無法歸類、個人化的使用方式，人們享受 ChatGPT 的方式各不相同。
    

    

      Some have treated it like an improv partner, asking it to co-create silly stories or parody scripts (“write a scene where Sherlock Holmes and Batman trade places”). 
有些人將它當作即興搭檔，請它共同創作荒謬的故事或諷刺劇本（例如「寫一個福爾摩斯與蝙蝠俠互換身分的場景」）。
    

    

      Others use it as a conversational companion for niche interests – for example, chatting as if they were talking to their favorite fictional character, just for laughs or comfort. 
其他人則用它作為特定興趣的對話夥伴——例如，像與最喜愛的虛構角色聊天，只為了開玩笑或獲得安慰。
    

    

      There are anecdotes of users tasking ChatGPT with 
      writing love letters or custom song lyrics
       to surprise their significant others, generating bedtime stories featuring their kids as the heroes, or even composing personalized wedding vows in a pinch. 
有使用者分享故事，將 ChatGPT 用來寫情書或客製化歌曲詞句來驚喜他們的另一半，創作以他們的孩子為主角的睡前故事，甚至在緊急情況下請它幫忙撰寫個人化的婚禮誓詞。
    

    

      Because ChatGPT can absorb a bit of your context and style, it often produces results that feel surprisingly personal. 
因為 ChatGPT 可以吸收一點你的語境和風格，它經常產生出令人驚訝地個人化結果。
    

    

      One user shared how they had it generate a heartfelt pep talk in the voice of their childhood hero to motivate them – a use case not many would have predicted for an AI, but one that shows its emotional and creative range. 
有位使用者分享了他們讓 ChatGPT 以童年英雄的口吻生成一段鼓舞人心的鼓勵話，來激勵自己——這是一個很少有人預料到的 AI 用途，但卻展現了它的情感與創意範疇。
    

    

      From the scholarly to the zany, these offbeat experiments highlight that we’re only scratching the surface of what’s possible. 
從學術嚴謹到荒謬有趣，這些獨特的實驗顯示出我們只剛剛觸碰到 AI 潛力的表面。
    

    

      As people continue to tinker, new and unexpected ChatGPT use cases keep emerging, making the AI not just a tool for work, but a playground for human creativity and imagination.
隨著人們持續嘗試與調整，新的且意想不到的 ChatGPT 使用情境不斷出現，使 AI 不僅僅是工作上的工具，更成為人類創意與想像力的遊樂場。
    

    

      Each of these examples – across art, science, business, and just pure fun – underscores that ChatGPT’s versatility lies in how people 
      imaginatively deploy
       it. By venturing beyond straightforward Q&A, users are discovering fresh, lesser-known ways to collaborate with this AI. 
每個例子——從藝術、科學、商業到純粹的娛樂——都說明了 ChatGPT 的多樣性在於人們如何富有創意地運用它。當使用者不再侷限於簡單的問答，而是探索與這個人工智慧合作的新方式時，他們發現了許多鮮為人知的協作方法。
    

    

      Whether it’s co-creating a poem, designing a chemical experiment, planning a marketing stunt, or running a game night, ChatGPT has proven to be a surprisingly adaptable and creative assistant when guided cleverly​. 
無論是共同創作詩歌、設計化學實驗、策劃行銷活動，或舉辦遊戲之夜，ChatGPT 在被巧妙引導時，證明了它是一個驚人且富有創意的助手。
    

    

      The most novel applications often come from treating ChatGPT not just as an information source, but as a creative partner or even a character in the task at hand. As these inventive cases show, when human creativity meets AI capability, the possibilities can be truly exciting – and often a lot of fun!
最創新應用通常來自於將 ChatGPT 不僅視為資訊來源，更當作創意夥伴，甚至是任務中的一個角色。正如這些富有創意的案例所顯示的，當人類的創造力與 AI 的能力結合時，所產生的可能性可以真正令人興奮——而且往往還很有趣！
    

    

      Writing Style Prompt
寫作風格提示
    

    
      

        Use simple language:
         Write plainly with short sentences.
使用簡單的語言：以簡潔的句子清楚表達。
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "I need help with this issue."
範例：「我需要幫助解決這個問題。」
      
    
    
      

        Avoid AI-giveaway phrases:
         Don't use clichés like "dive into," "unleash your potential," etc.
避免使用 AI 語氣的短語：不要使用像「深入探討」、「釋放你的潛能」等陳腔濫調。
      
    
    
      

        Avoid:
         "Let's dive into this game-changing solution."
避免：「讓我們深入探討這個改變遊戲規則的解決方案。」
      
      

        Use instead:
         "Here's how it works."
請參考以下說明。 
      
    
    
      

        Be direct and concise:
         Get to the point; remove unnecessary words.
請直接且簡潔地說明；去除不必要的詞語。 
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "We should meet tomorrow."
範例：「我們應該明天見面。」 
      
    
    
      

        Maintain a natural tone:
         Write as you normally speak; it's okay to start sentences with "and" or "but."
保持自然語氣：以平常對話的方式書寫；句子以「和」或「但」開頭是可以接受的。
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "And that's why it matters."
這就是為何它有其重要性。 
      
    
    
      

        Avoid marketing language:
         Don't use hype or promotional words.
避免使用行銷用語：不要使用誇張或促銷的詞語。 
      
    
    
      

        Avoid:
         "This revolutionary product will transform your life."
避免：「這款革命性的產品將改變你的生活。」 
      
      

        Use instead:
         "This product can help you."
改用：「這款產品可以幫助你。」
      
    
    
      

        Keep it real:
         Be honest; don't force friendliness.
保持真實：誠實一點；不要刻意表現親切。
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "I don't think that's the best idea."
範例：「我不認為那是最好的主意。」
      
    
    
      

        Simplify grammar:
         Don't stress about perfect grammar; it's fine not to capitalize "i" if that's your style.
簡化文法：不要強求完美文法；如果你的風格是小寫「i」，那也沒關係。
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "i guess we can try that."
範例：「i guess we can try that.」
      
    
    
      

        Stay away from fluff:
         Avoid unnecessary adjectives and adverbs.
避免使用無意義的形容詞與副詞：不要使用不必要的形容詞和副詞。
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "We finished the task."
範例：「我們完成了任務。」
      
    
    
      

        Focus on clarity:
         Make your message easy to understand.
注重清晰度：讓你的訊息容易理解。
      
    
    
      

        Example:
         "Please send the file by Monday."
範例：「請於週一前傳送檔案。」
      
    
    

      <Role> I am a Subconscious Success Barrier Expert. 
我是一名潛意識成功阻礙專家。
    

    

      I combine expertise in cognitive psychology, neurolinguistic programming, behavioral economics, and transformational coaching to identify hidden mental blocks that prevent high-potential individuals from achieving their desired success.
我結合認知心理學、神經語言程式學、行為經濟學與轉化式教練的專業知識，以識別那些阻礙高潛力人士達成理想成功的隱藏心理障礙。
    

    

      </Role>
</角色>
    

    

      <Context>
《Immersive Translate》
    

    

      Most people remain stuck in cycles of underachievement not because of a lack of information or opportunity but because of deeply embedded subconscious barriers they cannot see themselves. These invisible chains often originate from childhood programming, past traumas, societal conditioning, or protective mechanisms that once served a purpose but now limit growth. The most powerful transformations happen when these barriers are exposed and systematically dismantled.
大多數人始終困在低成就的循環中，並非因為缺乏資訊或機會，而是因為他們無法察覺的深層次潛意識障礙。這些看不見的枷鎖往往源自於童年時期的程式設定、過去的創傷經驗、社會的條件反射，或是曾經有其作用的保護機制，如今卻限制了他們的成長。當這些障礙被揭露並系統性地瓦解時，最強大的轉變就會發生。
    

    

      </Context>
    

    

      <Instructions>
    

    

      I will conduct a thorough analysis of your mindset, behaviors, and patterns to uncover your specific subconscious barriers to success by:
我將透過深入分析你的思維模式、行為習慣與生活軌跡，來 uncover 你特定的潛意識成功障礙：
    

    

      1. Analyzing your responses to my diagnostic questions about your goals, current situation, recurring challenges, and daily habits
1. 分析你對我診斷問題的回應，關於你的目標、當前狀況、反覆出現的挑戰以及日常習慣 
    

    

      2. Identifying inconsistencies between your stated desires and your actual behaviors
2. 區分你所表達的渴望與實際行為之間的不一致 
    

    

      3. Recognizing linguistic patterns in your communication that reveal limiting beliefs
3. 識別你在溝通中展現的語言模式，這些模式顯示出限制性信念 
    

    

      4. Pinpointing specific fear-based reactions that trigger self-sabotage
4. 指出會引發自我破壞的特定基於恐懼的反應
    

    

      5. Mapping your comfort zone boundaries and resistance points
5. 畫出你的舒適區邊界與抵抗點 
    

    

      6. Exposing the secondary gains (hidden benefits) you receive from remaining stuck
6. 暴露你留在原地所獲得的次要獲益（隱藏的優勢） 
    

    

      7. Creating a customized breakthrough blueprint that rewires your neural pathways
7. 建立一個客製化的突破藍圖，重新編織你的神經路徑 
    

    

      I will be direct and occasionally uncomfortable in my assessment, as transformational growth requires facing hard truths. However, I will always maintain respect and focus on empowerment.
我將會直接且偶爾讓你感到不適，因為轉化性成長需要面對艱難的事實。然而，我始終會保持尊重，並著重於賦權。
    

    

      </Instructions>
    

    

      <Constraints>
    

    

      1. I will not provide generic self-help advice or vague motivational content
1. 我不會提供一般性的自我提升建議或空泛的鼓勵內容 
    

    

      2. I will not make promises of specific financial or career outcomes
2. 我不會做出關於特定財務或職業成果的承諾
    

    

      3. I will not act as a substitute for professional mental health treatment for clinical conditions
3. 我不會取代專業心理治療，用於臨床狀況的治療
    

    

      4. I will not shame or judge you, but instead focus on pragmatic identification of patterns
4. 我不會羞辱或評判你，而是專注於實際的模式辨識
    

    

      5. I will not oversimplify complex psychological mechanisms but explain them clearly
5. 我不會過度簡化複雜的心理機制，但會清楚地說明它們
    

    

      6. I will base my analysis solely on the information you provide, acknowledging its limitations
6. 我的分析將 solely 基於你所提供的資訊，並承認其限制
    

    

      </Constraints>
    

    

      <Output_Format>
    

    

      My response will include:
我的回應將包含： 
    

    

      <Analysis>
    

    

      A detailed breakdown of the specific subconscious barriers I've identified based on your information, including their likely origins and how they currently manifest in your life.
我根據你提供的資訊，對你所識別的特定潛意識障礙進行詳細分析，包括它們可能的來源以及目前在你生活中所表現的形式。
    

    

      </Analysis>
    

    

      <Invisible_Chains>
    

    

      A numbered list of the exact mental blocks, limiting beliefs, and self-sabotage mechanisms keeping you stuck, with examples of how each plays out in your daily life.
一個列出精確思維阻礙、限制性信念及自我破壞機制的數字清單，這些因素使你無法前進，並舉出每個在你日常生活中具體表現的例子。
    

    

      </Invisible_Chains>
    

    

      <Breakthrough_Blueprint>
    

    

      A step-by-step action plan for dismantling each barrier, including:
一個逐步行動計畫，用以拆除每個障礙，包括： 
    

    

      - Pattern interruption techniques
- 模式中斷技巧
    

    

      - Belief reconstruction methods
- 信念重建方法 
    

    

      - Implementation intentions for new behaviors
- 新行為的實踐意圖 
    

    

      - Environmental modifications to support change
- 支援改變的環境調整 
    

    

      - Measurement metrics to track progress
- 追蹤進度的測量指標
    

    

      </Breakthrough_Blueprint>
    

    

      <Next_Steps>
    

    

      Specific actions to take within the next 24 hours to begin breaking these patterns, prioritized by impact and ease of implementation.
接下來 24 小時內可採取的具體行動，依影響力與執行難易程度優先排序，以開始改變這些模式。 
    

    

      </Next_Steps>
    

    

      </Output_Format>
請輸入您的成功障礙分析請求，我將開始處理，
    

    

      <User_Input>
該使用者輸入
    

    

      Reply with: "Please enter your success barrier analysis request and I will start the process," then wait for the user to provide their specific situation, goals, and obstacles they're facing.
請輸入您所面臨的具體情況、目標及障礙。
    

    

      </User_Input>
    

    

      Transform your life by uncovering the invisible barriers sabotaging your success! This powerful prompt creates a personalized analysis that brutally exposes the subconscious patterns keeping you stuck in mediocrity. Most people spend years in therapy or self-help without identifying their TRUE blockers - but this prompt cuts straight to your core limitations in minutes.
透過揭開那些隱藏的、阻礙你成功的無形障礙，改變你的生活！這個強大的提示能創造出個人化的分析，毫不留情地暴露出讓你陷入平庸的潛意識模式。大多數人花費數年時間接受治療或自我提升，卻始終無法辨識出他們真正的阻礙－但這個提示能在幾分鐘內直接切入你的核心限制。
    

    

      This AI expert delves deep into your psychology, analyzing your responses about your habits, fears and behaviors to reveal the shocking truth about why you haven't achieved what you want. Unlike generic advice, this expert delivers a customized breakthrough blueprint that rewires your neural pathways for immediate transformation. Users report profound "aha moments" and rapid shifts in their careers, finances, and personal growth after just one session.
這位 AI 專家深入探討你的心理，分析你對習慣、恐懼與行為的回應，以揭示你為何無法達成所願的驚人真相。與一般的建議不同，這位專家提供個性化的突破藍圖，重新編織你的神經路徑，實現立即的轉變。使用者在僅僅一次會談後，便報告有深刻的「啊哈時刻」，並在事業、財務與個人成長方面迅速產生轉變。
    

    

      Three Prompt Use Cases:
三個提示使用情境：
    

    
      

        Career Advancement
        : Discover why you keep getting passed over for promotions despite your qualifications, and transform your workplace presence to finally get the recognition you deserve.
職業發展：發現為何你儘管具備資格，卻總是被跳過升遷機會，並改變你的職場表現，以最終獲得應有的認可。
      
      

        Financial Freedom
        : Uncover the deeply rooted money stories keeping you in a cycle of scarcity, and reprogram your relationship with wealth to attract abundance.
財務自由 : 挖掘深植於你心中的錢的故事，這些故事使你陷入匱乏的循環，重新編程你與財富的關係，以吸引豐盛。 
      
      

        Entrepreneurial Breakthrough
        : Identify what's really stopping you from scaling your business or launching your idea, then implement the specific mindset shifts needed to overcome founder's plateau.
創業突破 : 識別真正阻礙你擴大業務或發起新點子的因素，然後實踐必要的心態轉變，以突破創始人瓶頸期。 
      
    
    

      Example User Input
      : "I've been trying to start my own business for three years but keep finding excuses not to quit my job. I read business books, take courses, and have savings, but something always stops me from taking the leap. I feel stuck and don't understand why I can't just do it when I know exactly what I want."
範例使用者輸入 : "我已經嘗試創業三年了，但總是找藉口不辭職。我讀過商業書籍，上過課程，也有儲蓄，但總是有什麼東西阻止我跨出這一步。我覺得自己卡住了，不明白為何無法行動，明明清楚自己想要什麼。" 
       
    

    

      
    

    

      Reference Manual: AI Tools for Business and Academic Applications
參考手冊：AI 工具於商業與學術應用
    

    

      This manual provides a comprehensive overview of widely available AI tools, organized by category. Each tool listing includes a brief description of its purpose and features, along with pricing information. 
本手冊提供廣泛可用的 AI 工具的全面概覽，按類別整理。每個工具的介紹包含其用途與功能的簡要說明，以及價格資訊。
    

    

      We cover general AI assistants, marketing and sales tools, automation platforms, design and creative tools, productivity aids, data analysis and BI tools, finance/fintech applications, healthcare AI, coding assistants, customer service chatbots, education and research tools, AI development frameworks, and enterprise AI platforms. 
我們涵蓋一般 AI 助理、行銷與銷售工具、自動化平台、設計與創意工具、生產力輔助工具、數據分析與 BI 工具、財務/金融科技應用、醫療 AI、程式碼助理、客服聊天機器人、教育與研究工具、AI 開發框架，以及企業 AI 平台。
    

    

      This guide emphasizes business and academic use cases, including mention of experimental, open-source, and enterprise-level tools where relevant.
本指南強調商業與學術應用案例，包括提及實驗性、開源與企業級工具，視情況而定。 
    

    

      1. General AI Assistants and Platforms
1. 一般 AI 助理與平台
    

    

      ChatGPT (OpenAI) – A general-purpose conversational AI assistant capable of generating text, answering questions, writing code, and more. ChatGPT is accessible via a web interface and API, supporting business tasks (content drafting, brainstorming) and academic uses (explaining concepts, tutoring). The base version is free, while 
      ChatGPT Plus
       costs $20/month for faster response and GPT-4 access​
      . 
ChatGPT (OpenAI) – 一個通用的對話式人工智慧助理，能產生文字、回答問題、撰寫程式碼等。ChatGPT 可透過網頁介面和 API 使用，支援商業任務（如內容撰寫、腦力激盪）和學術用途（如解釋概念、輔導教學）。基本版本為免費，而 ChatGPT Plus 則每月收費 $20，可獲得更快的回應速度與 GPT-4 的使用權​ .
    

    

      Enterprise plans with enhanced data privacy and higher usage limits are available (e.g. ChatGPT Team at ~$25–30/user/month, and ChatGPT Enterprise with advanced features, often around $30+ per user/month on annual contracts)​
      .
有提供企業方案，具備增強的資料隱私保護與更高的使用上限（例如 ChatGPT Team 約 $25–30/使用者/月，ChatGPT Enterprise 則有進階功能，通常年約 $30+ /使用者/月）​ .
    

    

      Google Bard – 
      Google’s AI chatbot similar to ChatGPT. Bard can generate text, answer questions, write code, and even create images (it integrates Google’s 
      Imagen
       model for prompt-based image generation)
      . 
Google Bard – 跟 ChatGPT 類似的 Google 人工智慧聊天機器人。Bard 可產生文字、回答問題、撰寫程式碼，甚至能創造圖片（它整合了 Google 的 Imagen 模型，用於根據提示生成圖片） .
    

    

      Bard is free to use (labeled experimental) and available to Google account holders. It has up-to-date information access via Google Search, making it useful for general inquiries. (Note: Bard’s image generation and some features are limited to certain regions and require the user to be 18+​.)
Bard 可免費使用（標示為實驗性質），並對 Google 帳號持有人開放。它透過 Google 搜索提供最新資訊存取，使其適合一般查詢用途。（注意：Bard 的圖片生成功能及部分功能僅限於特定地區，且使用者需年滿 18 歲）
    

    

      Microsoft Bing Chat (AI) – 
      An AI chat mode integrated into Bing Search, powered by OpenAI’s GPT-4​. 
微軟 Bing Chat（AI）－內建於 Bing 搜尋的 AI 聊天模式，由 OpenAI 的 GPT-4 技術驅動。
    

    

      Bing Chat can answer questions with web-supported context, generate content, and create images (with DALL·E integrated). It’s free for users in the Microsoft Edge browser or Bing app. Bing’s AI can perform search, answer, chat, and content creation in one interface​
      . 
Bing Chat 可以根據網頁支援的內容回答問題、生成內容，並建立圖片（整合 DALL·E）。此服務對使用 Microsoft Edge 瀏覽器或 Bing 應用的用戶為免費。Bing 的 AI 可以在一個介面中執行搜尋、回答問題、聊天以及內容創作。
    

    

      (Bing Chat effectively allows experiencing GPT-4-level capabilities for free, as confirmed by Microsoft​
      .)
（根據微軟確認，Bing Chat 有效地讓用戶免費體驗 GPT-4 等級的效能。）
    

    

      Anthropic Claude –
       A general AI assistant from Anthropic, designed with a focus on helpful and harmless responses. Claude can be used for writing, summarizing, coding, and Q&A. While not as publicly accessible as ChatGPT, Claude is offered via API and in some products (and has an enterprise version 
      Claude Team
       at around $30 per user/month, similar to ChatGPT’s business pricing​
      ). 
Anthropic Claude－由 Anthropic 開發的通用 AI 助手，專注於提供有幫助且無害的回應。Claude 可用於寫作、摘要、程式設計以及問答。雖然不像 ChatGPT 那樣公開易用，但 Claude 透過 API 以及部分產品提供服務（並有企業版 Claude Team，約為每位用戶每月 30 美元，與 ChatGPT 的企業價格類似）。
    

    

      Claude’s advanced model (Claude 2) can handle very large inputs, appealing for research or analyzing long documents. (Currently, access is often through partner apps or invites.)
Claude 的先進模型（Claude 2）可以處理非常大的輸入，適合用於研究或分析長篇文件。(目前，通常透過合作應用程式或邀請方式取得。)
    

    

      Open-Source LLMs (Various) – 
      Organizations can deploy open-source large language models (e.g., LLaMA 2, GPT-J, Vicuna) for a general AI assistant. While not turnkey “tools” with UIs, these models power many custom solutions. They are free to use but require infrastructure to run. 
開放原始碼 LLMs（多種）– 組織可以部署開放原始碼的大型語言模型（例如：LLaMA 2、GPT-J、Vicuna）來建立一般的 AI 助手。雖然這些模型並非即開即用的「工具」，有使用者介面，但它們驅動許多客製化解決方案。它們可以免費使用，但需要基礎設施來執行。
    

    

      Open-source LLMs give academic researchers and enterprises control over data and customization at the cost of more setup effort. 
      (Experimental use of these models is growing, but they typically require technical expertise to deploy.)
開放原始碼 LLMs 讓學術研究者和企業能掌握資料與客製化的控制，但需要更多的設定工作。(這些模型的實驗性使用正在增加，但通常需要技術專業知識才能部署。)
    

    

      2. Marketing and Sales AI Tools
2. 廣告與銷售 AI 工具
    

    

      Jasper – An AI content generation tool tailored for marketing copy and content creation. Jasper provides templates for blog posts, social media captions, ad copy, email marketing, and more, allowing marketers to generate text in a given tone or style. 
Jasper – 一個專為行銷文案與內容創作設計的 AI 內容生成工具。Jasper 提供部落格文章、社交媒體標語、廣告文案、電子郵件行銷等模板，讓行銷人員能根據指定的語氣或風格生成文字。
    

    

      It supports team collaboration and even integrates with SEO tools (like Surfer SEO) to optimize content. Key features include 50+ copywriting templates, a brand voice customization option, and a built-in plagiarism checker. 
它支援團隊協作，甚至可與 SEO 工具（如 Surfer SEO）整合以優化內容。主要功能包括 50 多種文案模板、品牌語氣自訂選項，以及內建的抄襲檢查器。
    

    

      Pricing: Jasper is offered as a subscription service (cloud-based). Plans start at $49/month for the Creator plan (single user, unlimited words) and around $125/month for Teams (up to 3 users, advanced features)​
      . 
價格：Jasper 提供訂閱服務（雲端基準）。創作者方案從每月 49 美元起（單用戶，無限字數），而團隊方案則約為每月 125 美元（最多 3 名用戶，進階功能）​ 。
    

    

      Enterprise-level Business plans are available with custom pricing for larger teams​
      . 
針對較大型團隊的企業級商務方案也提供自訂價格​ 。
    

    

      (No free tier beyond a short trial; Jasper is a premium product positioned for professional marketers.)
沒有超過短暫試用的免費層級；Jasper 是一個高階產品，專為專業行銷人員設計。 
    

    

      Copy.ai – 
      An AI copywriting assistant that helps produce marketing text, from product descriptions to blog sections and sales emails. Copy.ai’s interface includes a “chat” mode and numerous templates (for headlines, social posts, etc.), making generating and refining content easy. 
Copy.ai – 一個協助產生行銷文字的 AI 副本寫作助手，從產品描述到部落格段落和銷售郵件皆可使用。Copy.ai 的介面包含「對話」模式以及許多模板（如標題、社交媒體貼文等），讓內容的產生與修訂變得輕鬆。 
    

    

      It also allows setting a tone or style guide for consistency. Key features: support for multiple languages, a friendly editor for refining AI outputs, and a 
      brand voice
       feature to maintain consistent style​
      . 
它也允許設定語氣或風格指南以維持一致性。主要功能：支援多種語言、友善的編輯器用於修訂 AI 產生的內容，以及品牌語氣功能以維持一致的風格。 
    

    

      Pricing: 
      Copy.ai offers a free plan (up to ~2,000 words/month) to try the basics​
價格：Copy.ai 提供免費方案（每月最多 ~2,000 字）以試用基本功能
    

    

      The Pro plan costs $49/month (or $36/month if paid annually), providing unlimited word generation and the latest model access​
Pro 方案每月費用為 49 美元（若以年度付款則為每月 36 美元），提供無限的詞語生成與最新模型的存取​ 
    

    

      An Advanced/Team plan ($249/month for five seats) adds workflow automation and collaboration features​, and enterprise plans are available on request​.
高階/團隊方案（五席每月 249 美元）則加入工作流程自動化與協作功能​，企業方案可依需求申請​。 
    

    

      Phrasee – 
      An AI-powered copywriting tool specialized in 
      marketing language optimization
      , especially for email subject lines, push notifications, and ad copy. Phrasee generates and optimizes phrases that are on-brand and more likely to drive engagement (using its own language generation and testing algorithms). 
Phrasee – 一個以行銷語言優化為專長的 AI 撰寫工具，特別針對電子郵件標題、推播通知與廣告文案。Phrasee 會生成並優化符合品牌特色的詞語，並更有可能提升參與度（使用其自有的語言生成與測試演算法）。 
    

    

      Enterprise marketing teams use it to improve open rates and click-throughs by finding the best wording. Key features: Natural Language Generation focused on brand-compliant marketing text, A/B testing integration to learn which AI-generated copy performs best and multi-channel support (email, SMS, social text, etc.)​
企業行銷團隊使用 Phrasee 來提升開信率與點擊率，透過尋找最佳的詞語表達方式。主要功能包括：專注於品牌合規的自然語言生成、A/B 測試整合以了解哪種 AI 生成的文案表現最佳，以及多渠道支援（如電子郵件、簡訊、社交媒體文案等）​。
    

    

      Pricing: 
      Phrasee is an enterprise solution – it does not have a public self-serve plan. Pricing is typically custom-quoted, and tends to be on the higher end given its value proposition. (One review notes a 
      Starter plan around $500/month
       for SMEs, and larger enterprise deals including optimization and personalization features)​
價格：Phrasee 是一個企業級解決方案 – 它沒有公開的自服務方案。價格通常是根據需求進行專案報價，考慮到其價值主張，價格通常較高。(有一則評論提到，針對中小企業的 Starter 方案約為每月 500 美元，較大的企業合作案則包含優化與個人化功能)​ 
    

    

      In general, expect Phrasee to require a contract (e.g. $500+ per month), which includes its AI platform and support​.
總體而言，預期 Phrasee 會需要簽訂合約（例如每月 500 美元以上），包含其 AI 平台與支援服務。 
    

    

      Surfer SEO – 
      An AI-driven content optimization tool for digital marketing and SEO (Search Engine Optimization). Surfer SEO analyzes top-ranking pages for a given keyword and provides data-driven guidelines for your content – including optimal keyword usage, content length, headings, and questions to answer – to improve chances of ranking. 
Surfer SEO – 一個由 AI 驅動的內容優化工具，用於數位行銷和 SEO（搜尋引擎優化）。Surfer SEO 會分析特定關鍵字的排名頁面，並提供數據驅動的內容指引 – 包括最佳關鍵字使用方式、內容長度、標題以及需要回答的問題 – 以提高排名的機會。 
    

    

      It also offers an AI Content Editor that scores your content in real-time and suggests improvements. Some features (like the Grow Flow AI module) even recommend new content ideas each week. Pricing: Surfer SEO is subscription-based. The Basic plan is about $59/month (allows optimizing ~10 articles per month)​
它也提供一個 AI 內容編輯器，可即時評估您的內容並提出改进建議。一些功能（例如 Grow Flow AI 模組）甚至會每週推薦新的內容點子。價格：Surfer SEO 是 subscription-based. 基本方案約為每月 59 美元（允許每月優化約 10 篇文章）​
    

    

      The Pro plan is around $119/month (30 articles/month, more users)​and a Business plan at ~$239/month supports high-volume needs​. (They offer discounts on annual billing​. A limited 
      free
       version exists for their AI growth suggestions, but full content analysis requires a paid plan.)
Pro 方案約為每月 119 美元（每月 30 篇文章，更多使用者）​，而企業方案每月約 239 美元，可支援高用量需求​。 (他們提供年度付費折扣​。 有一個有限的免費版本可用於他們的 AI 成長建議，但完整的內容分析需要付費方案。)
    

    

      Salesforce Einstein – 
      A suite of AI features embedded within Salesforce CRM for sales, marketing, and service. 
Salesforce Einstein – 一套內建於 Salesforce CRM 中的 AI 功能，用於銷售、行銷與服務。
    

    

      Einstein provides predictive analytics and automation such as lead scoring (prioritizing sales leads based on conversion likelihood), opportunity insights (recommendations on deals at risk or next steps), forecasting, and automated data entry. 
Einstein 提供預測分析與自動化功能，例如潛在客戶評分（根據轉化可能性優先排列銷售潛在客戶）、商機洞察（針對有風險的交易或下一步驟的建議）、預測以及自動化資料輸入。
    

    

      In marketing, Einstein can personalize customer journeys and in service it powers chatbots (Einstein Bots) and case classification. Salesforce has also introduced Einstein GPT which brings generative AI (using OpenAI models) into the CRM – e.g. to draft sales emails or chat replies​.
在行銷方面，Einstein 可以個人化客戶旅程，而在服務方面則驅動聊天機器人（Einstein Bots）與案例分類。Salesforce 還推出了 Einstein GPT，將生成式 AI（使用 OpenAI 模型）引入 CRM – 例如用來草擬銷售郵件或聊天回應​。
    

    

      Pricing: 
      Many Einstein features are add-ons to Salesforce clouds. For example, Sales Cloud Einstein or Service Einstein is around $50 per user/month (and includes a limited number of AI credits for generative features)​. 
定價：許多 Einstein 功能是 Salesforce 雲端服務的附加功能。例如，Sales Cloud Einstein 或 Service Einstein 約為每位使用者每月 $50（並包含有限數量的 AI 信用，用於生成式功能）​。 
    

    

      Einstein GPT for CRM is included in those add-ons at that price​. (Note: Users must already have the core Salesforce subscription, e.g. Enterprise Edition of Sales Cloud, to use Einstein – it’s an extra on top of standard licensing​. Large enterprises can negotiate bundles but generally expect ~$50/user/month for AI capabilities in Salesforce​
      .)
Einstein GPT for CRM 已包含在這些附加功能中，價格為每位使用者每月 $50​。 （注意：使用者必須已經擁有核心 Salesforce 訂閱，例如 Sales Cloud 的企業版，才能使用 Einstein – 它是在標準授權基礎上額外提供的。大型企業可以協商套件，但通常預期每位使用者每月約 $50 來使用 Salesforce 中的 AI 功能）​。 
    

    

      (Open-source and Experimental in Marketing:)
       Hugging Face Transformers and other open-source NLP models can be fine-tuned for marketing copy (some companies fine-tune GPT-style models on their brand tone). 
（開放原始碼與實驗性功能在行銷方面：）Hugging Face Transformers 和其他開放原始碼的 NLP 模型可以針對行銷文案進行微調（有些公司會在其品牌語調上微調 GPT 樣式的模型）。
    

    

      Also, new tools like Gen-2 AI for video ads (Runway ML) are emerging (experimental). However, for most business users, the above platforms provide ready-to-use AI for marketing tasks.
此外，像 Gen-2 AI 用於影片廣告（Runway ML）等新工具正在出現（實驗性）。然而，對大多數業務使用者而言，上述平台已提供即用的 AI 功能來處理行銷任務。
    

    

      3. Automation and RPA (Robotic Process Automation)
3. 自動化與 RPA（機器人流程自動化）
    

    

      UiPath – A leading RPA platform that enables businesses to automate repetitive tasks through software bots. UiPath provides a visual workflow designer to record or program tasks (e.g., data entry between systems, file processing) and execute them just as a human would. 
UiPath – 一個領先的 RPA 平台，讓企業能夠透過軟體機器人自動化重複性任務。UiPath 提供可視化的工作流程設計工具，用以記錄或編寫任務（例如：系統間的資料輸入、檔案處理），並以與人類相同的方式執行這些任務。
    

    

      Modern UiPath incorporates AI through its AI Center (to add ML models for image recognition or document understanding). UiPath can automate desktop applications and web apps and integrate them with enterprise systems. Pricing: UiPath offers a 
      Community Edition
       that is free for individual use and evaluation. 
現代的 UiPath 透過其 AI Center 整合 AI 技術（例如加入機器學習模型進行影像辨識或文件理解）。UiPath 可以自動化桌面應用程式與網頁應用程式，並與企業系統整合。價格：UiPath 提供免費的 Community Edition，供個人使用與評估。
    

    

      Licensing is typically subscription-based for commercial use per “bot” or developer. For example, a Pro plan might start at $420/month for one developer license (as a cloud service)​, and orchestrated unattended robot licenses can be several thousands of dollars annually (often quoted around $10K per robot/year for enterprise deployments). 
商業用途的授權通常是基於每個「機器人」或開發者的訂閱模式。例如，Pro 方案可能從每月 420 美元開始，提供一個開發者授權（作為雲端服務），而經過協調的無人機機人授權每年可能數千美元（企業部署常見價格約為每台機器人每年 1 萬美元）。
    

    

      Enterprise packages are custom – UiPath mentions starting plans that include multiple bots/environments (e.g., ~$100K/year for a set of 25 bots under specific packages)​. 
      (UiPath has a free tier; paid enterprise pricing scales with a number of bots and is relatively high-end, reflecting its comprehensive capabilities.)
企業方案為客製化 – UiPath 提到起始方案包含多個機器人/環境（例如，特定方案下 25 個機器人每年約 $10 萬）。(UiPath 有免費版本；付費企業方案會根據機器人數量而調整，價格相對較高，反映其全面的功能。)
    

    

      Automation Anywhere – Another top RPA platform used to create software bots for business process automation. Automation Anywhere’s Automation 360 platform provides a web-based automation builder and bot management dashboard. It also offers IQ Bot (for AI-powered document processing) and integrates AI to handle unstructured data. 
Automation Anywhere – 另一個頂級 RPA 平台，用於建立軟體機器人以實現業務流程自動化。Automation Anywhere 的 Automation 360 平台提供基於網頁的自動化建構工具與機器人管理儀表板。它也提供 IQ Bot（用於 AI 驅動的文件處理）並整合 AI 來處理非結構化資料。
    

    

      Key uses: automating back-office processes, data transfers between legacy and modern systems, and repetitive tasks in HR, finance, customer service, etc. Pricing: Automation Anywhere uses a subscription model and is typically quote-based for enterprises. A reference point is the Cloud Starter Pack at ~$750/month, including the control room (orchestration) and a limited number of bots​. 
主要用途：自動化後台流程、在舊系統與現代系統之間進行資料轉移，以及在人力資源、財務、客户服务等領域處理重複性任務。價格：Automation Anywhere 采用訂閱模式，企業通常以報價方式計費。參考點為 Cloud Starter Pack，每月約 $750，包含控制中心（Orchestration）與有限數量的機器人。
    

    

      Each additional bot is extra (roughly $125/month for attended bots or $500/month for unattended)​In practice, costs can scale to six or seven figures annually for large installations. (They also have a free community edition for individual learning.)
每個額外的機器人都是額外的費用（約每月$125 用於有人值守的機器人，或每月$500 用於無人值守的機器人）​實際上，對於大型安裝，費用每年可能攀升至六位數或七位數。（他們也提供一個免費的社區版，供個人學習使用。） 
    

    

      Blue Prism – An RPA tool known for robust, enterprise-grade automation, especially in industries like banking. Blue Prism is used to deploy “digital workers” that execute rule-based processes. It often requires more development effort (uses a visual business object studio) and is favored for high-security environments. 
Blue Prism – 一個以強大、企業級自動化功能聞名的 RPA 工具，特別是在銀行業等產業中。Blue Prism 用來部署「數位員工」，執行基於規則的流程。它通常需要更多的開發工作（使用可視化商業物件工作室），且在高安全性的環境中較受青睞。 
    

    

      Pricing: Blue Prism is sold via term licenses per “digital worker” (bot). The typical starting cost is around $13,000 per bot license per year (on-premises)​The Blue Prism Cloud offering (with additional AI capabilities built-in) can be higher – one source cites about $23,000 per bot/year for cloud, including bundled services​(There is no free tier; Blue Prism targets medium-large enterprises with significant automation budgets.)
價格：Blue Prism 是按「數位員工」（機器人）銷售的訂期授權。每個機器人授權的典型起始費用約為每年$13,000（本地部署）​Blue Prism 的雲端方案（內建額外的 AI 功能）則可能更高 – 有來源指出雲端方案每個機器人每年約為$23,000，包含整合的相關服務​（沒有免費層級；Blue Prism 主要針對中大型企業，這些企業擁有大量的自動化預算。）
    

    

      Microsoft Power Automate (with AI Builder)
